Page 23

電影專刊

（城市之夜）的喊呐

— 嘉炎

戲劇和電影的重要成份是（暗示）没有暗示，一張片子即使有良好的表演，也不過一朶朝開暮謝的藝術之花。有良好的表現，加以强有力的暗示的戲劇，才有永存性。城市之　夜，有深刻的暗示丨！平均地權。

城市的建築，是有義務而無權利者做成。城市的文明，是有權利而無義務者享樂。城市發逹以後，物價的飛漲，地産的抬高，把城市做成者丨！貧苦工人驅逐出境。而讓城市享樂者丨！紳士太太們丨！一切據爲己有。貧苦工人們，何嘗願意離開自已有血汗功勞的城市，怎奈（城市不易居）呢！那就是城市之夜的喊呐丨！

倘若有十幾處小房子别墅，公館，而每夜分身不下的老爺們，會想到貧無立錐的苦工。倘若穿百多元一件的來路羊毛背心，獺皮大衣，而打士汀爐傍邊打噴嚏的少爺們，，想到破棉被還在當舖廟未贖出來的窮骨頭。倘若天天赴宴而至不消化，生胃病，牙齒痛的闊佬，會想到餐粥餐飯的餓鬼。倘若姨太太多而至神筋衰的大漢，會想到餓死老婆的窮鬼，那就好了。貧富衝突可以和解了。共産的恐怖至少可以遲到五十年了。可惜有錢有勢的大人先生們没想到這一層！獨善其身的人太多了。兼善大衆的人太少了。他們爲己的精神太專注了。竟忘却改進社會，爲大衆謀幸福，爲人羣减輕痛苦，是每個有錢有勢的大人先生們的責任。而且只有他們才有這種力量丨！否則貧富不均，苦樂懸殊的現狀愈顯著，貧富的衝突愈猛烈，勢必趨向同歸於盡的途徑！

雖然城市中不少爲富兼仁的大慈善家，大活佛。可是總覺得杯水車薪，無濟於事。慈善事業，是要用科學方法才有普及的效果。在馬路上分錢給以叩頭爲職業的乞丐，反爲增加他們的依賴心。施粥施飯，救得一時救不得一世。最完善，最經濟，最永久的慈善事業，就是復興工廠。受日本的砲毁，和不景氣的打擊，工廠停了不少。工人失業的不得了。須知工廠一日不復開，不重建，富翁不過少賺一日錢。但是工人却少食一日飯。富翁們恐怕賺不到錢，便不敢開工廠。而願意倒貼利息存入外國銀行，或者經營地産，提高地價，加重貧民房租的負擔，實行（率土地而食人肉）的致富術！同一樣想賺錢，爲甚麽不肯做有益人羣的企業，而偏要做損人利已的治産呢？倘若富富翁們肯投資工廠，那麽不獨國内工業可以發逹，而且貧民可以有自食其力的機會，一家飽煖，自然没有爲非作列的事。那眞是修子修孫，功德無量的好事啊！

觀衆意見

評（一剪梅）

— 椀

（一剪梅）曾經在（中央）映過，今天又在西海放映，上座不多。

嚴格說起來，這張片子，荒謬的地方甚多。舉出來，讓大衆評題一下！

白樂德是一個脂粉將軍，卑鄙小人，胡倫廷旣然在學校裏頭都看不起他，怎麽會和他結交，况且初到人家，就窺人内宅，調戲人家的閨閫，這種下流行徑，胡倫廷是深曉得他的，怎樣臨走的時候，倒把妹妹託這種人照應呢？

二，胡麗珠入手就看不起白樂德，後來白樂德傾陷她胞兄的陰謀工又發覺了，到底麗珠還是和他結婚，大槪這也是呌做（孽緣）吧？

三，軍閥的小姐當衛隊長，這種胡調，未免太不近情。

此外可笑的地方還多，不能一一提出。倒是演員方面，却個個都很成就。除掉王次龍的擠眉弄眼，稍爲過火之外，阮玲玉的麗珠，自首至尾，無懈可擊。還有攝影方面，也算不差，幾幕美術風景，亦甚出色，因此下了這張片子的總評一句，就是（演員很好，導演太差）。

評（體貼入微）

— 梅邨

當我看外國片時，每每感到劇情不緊奏而看得莫明其妙，在這（體貼入微）裏，劇情很連貫，没有讀說明書，也能懂得内容，所以該片的導演在劇情分幕的安排上，已免掉不緊凑的弊病。

男主角吉姆士鄧飾少年律師皮爾，以主角地位言，僅能說平常稱職，没有驚人的表演，女主角蒲絲瑪洛蘭飾一淑女海倫，聽說還是第一次上鏡頭，態度閒雅，誠屬難得，對於愛護她姊姊遺下的兩個孩子，在湯曼驚夢呌喊一幕内，盡露慈愛之懷，却到好處，飾二個小孩的裴斯德菲爾士和喬琪安斯納均很好，一種天眞瀾漫的自然態度，極有精彩，可說能幕幕討人歡喜，也是全劇最生色之處。

當却利從窗口逃出而喊集千百孩童，圍住玻爾寓所一幕，穿插很妙，是全劇最緊張的地方，其他像大百貨商店的情形，簡單的分幕演出，適合需要，不覺什麽麻煩，也是滿意。

以劇情言，原是一部男女愛情片，而在父母愛子的表情上，也有深刻的描摹，所以不獨在男女愛情上可說（體貼入微），即在父母愛子和孩子愛他的父母上，也能見到（體貼入微），這片是該的劇名和劇情有兼顧吻合之妙呀。

蕭伯納諷嘲好萊塢

— 華明

愛爾蘭諷剌作家蕭伯納氏此次環遊世界過美國時，好萊塢影片藝術科學研究學院特預先以長途電話請蕭氏赴好萊塢攝一二短片，蕭氏當於電話中答稱（演講且曾聲明謝絶，何况攝片？）後雷電華派拉蒙及華納第一國家三公司聨名派代表與蕭氏面商，請蕭氏至少須攝一小段短片，蕭氏笑答曰：（蕭函納老矣，設或年少翩翩，則定來博一美男子之名，毋須諸君之請矣，）諸代表猶婉言懇函：片蕭氏又曰：）蕭函納酷愛金錢，恐至好萊塢後，雖驅之亦不肯離去。）云云，寥寥數語駡煞一般財奴矣。

數年以前，米同梅公司老闆塞茂高爾温氏，遊歐州，至英國時，曾請蕭伯納編一劇本，並聲明願出重金。蕭伯納答曰：一蕭伯納祇知金錢，不知有藝術，高爾温先生爲吾虚名所誤矣。）高爾温默然而退。

蕭伯納素不滿美國人所謂之（洋錢人）ＤｏｌｌａｒＭａｎ，尤痛恨好萊塢人物之恃財凌人，故其著作中戲劇雖多，未嘗貪金錢而將攝片權售於好萊塢云。

天一新片（追求）之一幕

攝（荒島情鴛）外景行期

— 墨客

在銀幕上己好久不見其出現的吳素馨，自其夫張惠民將華劇公司改爲惠民公司之後，繼（十九路軍光榮史）一片的（荒島情鴛，）籌備了好久，而内景也早己攝完，本定七日偕主要角色，往暹邏

洪深將重上影塲　趙鵬

戲劇家洪深君，自導演（女書記）一劇後久已放棄導演工作，近復徇明星影片公司張石川之請，將重登影塲，導演一新片（鐵版紅影錄，）以四川軍閥之横暴爲題材，表演軍閥禍國的情形，已選定陳凝秋君與王瑩女士充任男女主角；副導演高梨痕沈西苓君，將于下星期開始拍攝，陳凝秋君爲前南國劇社社員、于（南歸二劇，表演極得社會上人士之贊美，想現身銀幕必有良好成績焉。

攝取外影，不料吳素馨突然患感冐症，延醫診察後，已日見痊愈，但受醫生囑付，謂病後須靜養數日，故往暹邏拍取外影時期，延宕於本月底，或四月初云。

安哈定將脫銀幕生活

— 黄影呆

在好萊塢，最近又傳出了一個警只的消息，說是安哈定Ａｎｎ　Ｈａｒｄｉｎｇ將要脫離銀幕生活了。好的合同在今年的四月中滿期，在雷開華公司方面，雖然有自四月起將續訂一年合同的消息，然而安哈定却在懷疑她能否被選而繼續，因爲公司方面，有裁减演員的消息，據說過去的成績，如果有特殊的成功者，才能繼續訂立合同不幸得很，安哈定據考慮的結果，並没有列入成功的演員之中。

電影小說

紅塵（Ｒｅｄ　Ｄｕｓｌ）（四）

— 桀克

（是不是這樣的銷磨良宵？）她以善於交際的模樣問他，但尼斯並不回答，老是看他的地圖。

（有没有東西吃？我肚子餓得要命！）這婦人埋怨地問。

（廚房在那後面。）他一仰頭示意。

（在西貢的時候，他們都說我消瘦了　　　您看我瘦了没有？）她下了桌子站在他面前。　　（我不管這此事，）但尼斯斬釘截鐵的回答，（請出去！）

（噯！唷！）葉丹向廚房走去，（可不必大驚小怪似的！出來幾天上又没法，要住一個月丨人家喝醉了酒丨大虫閙得您睡不着覺丨在客堂裏對大猩猩逗趣講好他可對您大驚小怪起來了：她自言自語的到了廚房，四週看着，瞥見了一匣餅乾，她伸手捻起匣子上面一個蟑鄉，（哈！）她胡調似的說，（你甚麽不在我的房間裏呢？）

她挾了一匣子餅乾回到客堂。那客堂已是聞其無人了。沿着陽台一個房間門開着射出燈光。但尼斯正在脫衣服。　丹拿出一塊餅乾就咀嚼。好遊目四顧，她的眼睛隨之表現出一種忽忽若有所失的神氣。在墻角。她瞥見一只鸚鵡在籠裏。

（噲，百俐，）她對牠逗趣着說。（同我講話丨我要尋一個人談談心呢！）那鳥對她　起一隻圓珠眼，然後咶啦咶啦的大笑起來了。蘩丹也頓時忍不住發出慘笑，並且拿一塊餅乾給鸚鵡。此後他們便成了要好朋友。

麥克見她口齒伶俐而不失天眞，日久也不免拜倒於她的天然美之下了。在居同遇分不對的時候，就是但尼斯也會袒護也的。

她把住宅的一事一物佈置得并然有條。夜晚和麥克門鬥牌的時候，她雖禁不住常常偷睨那無動乎中的但尼斯，她却並不更進一步去打動他的情緒。她很愉快的處理日常家務。一天但尼斯使着性告訴她說她可以拿（鸚鵡太太）去，她的眼睛便頓時融化了，她不曉得怎樣謝他，而他呢却一言不發的走了房子。

（知道，麥克，我不想回去呀，）蘩丹突然熱心的說。（不），她温柔說。（這四星期的時光好像（種香！異香。）

蘩丹在碼頭上看見但尼斯，他是來歡迎新到的工程師的。她對他喊。

（是不是來同我話别的？）好熱心地問。

他轉身走到她面前，第一次對她微微的笑。

（再會，孩子，）他拍拍她的手臂。（未完）

1933.03.22

Our Troops Firmly Defend Positions, Many Officers Killed and Wounded

Song Zheyuan Rushes to the Front Lines, Enemy Retreats North of Luowenyu

Beiping, Xifengkou Telephone Dispatch: Today at dawn, the enemy, numbering over three thousand, consisting of infantry and cavalry units, as well as combined Mongol and Korean troops, used heavy artillery and ten aircraft for cover, launching a fierce attack on the front of our Xifengkou position. The enemy bombarded our position with concentrated fire. Our soldiers remained hidden in trenches. After the enemy's aircraft and heavy artillery bombardment, large formations of the enemy aggressively advanced towards our position. Our troops waited until they were close, then suddenly leaped out of the trenches and engaged the enemy in fierce hand-to-hand combat for a long time. The enemy could not prevail and retreated. Our army continues to firmly hold the position. In this battle, our battalion commander was wounded, three company and platoon leaders were killed in action, and over a hundred soldiers were killed and wounded. It is anticipated that a major battle will occur at Xifengkou. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, After receiving news this morning that the enemy on the front of Xifengkou had reinforced their troops and launched a counterattack, Song Zheyuan immediately returned to the front lines of Xifengkou this afternoon by car to supervise the battle. Before departing, he discussed all military plans in detail with He Yingqin. Before leaving, Song told others that the Japanese army would engage in a fierce battle with us in the near future to wash away the humiliation of their defeat at Xifengkou and to conclude their offensive operations in Rehe. We have taken strict precautions, and the Xifengkou position has been built up. The enemy will definitely not succeed. (21st Dispatch)

Tianjin, According to reports, the enemy used 15,000 fresh troops, 20 tanks, and 20 armored vehicles, covered by artillery and aircraft, to launch a fierce attack on our Dongjiakou, Panjiakou, and Xifengkou positions on the afternoon of the 20th. In order to avoid enemy artillery fire, our troops have established a new defense line in the area, linking up with a certain unit at Lengkou to the right, and echoing the division at Longjingyu and Luowenyu to the left. The situation at the front is extremely critical. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, Zhang Zizhong and Li Wentian sent a telegram from here on the 20th stating that at 3:00 PM today, the enemy used eight aircraft and artillery near Baitai to bombard and cover their approximately 2,000 infantry troops, launching a fierce attack on the front of our Banjialing regiment. Our regimental commander led the first and second battalions of his regiment in a desperate resistance, ordering the third battalion to encircle the enemy's flank. After four hours of fierce fighting, including three or four hand-to-hand combats, the enemy was finally defeated and fled towards Tiemen and Dongjiakou. In this battle, He Guangqi, commander of the second company, Li Yunxuan, commander of the tenth company, Kong Xiangui, commander of the twelfth company, and platoon leaders Gao Yulong, Xu Menglan, and Wang Guoxian were killed in action. Battalion commander Yang Gan was wounded, and over two hundred soldiers were killed and wounded. (21st Dispatch)

Tianjin, This morning, enemy cavalry attacked the position of our brigade outside Dongjiakou but were repulsed by our troops. At 10:00 AM this morning, twelve enemy aircraft flew to Santunying, Saheqiao, and Zunhua, dropping bombs, wounding over twenty of our soldiers and civilians. The remnants of the enemy at Luowenyu retreated to the Banbishan area and are building new positions. Enemy reinforcements are continuously arriving, planning another general offensive. (21st Dispatch)

Tianjin, The enemy who attacked our Luowenyu on the 19th suffered heavy losses due to our encircling attack and retreated north on the morning of the 20th to the Banbishan and Foye Temple area. On the evening of the 20th, they again attacked our Luowenyu, Shancha, and other passes, resulting in fierce fighting throughout the night. On the morning of the 21st, they were again repulsed by our troops. It has been observed that the enemy retreats during the day and returns at night. It is heard that the enemy's rear has been moving towards a certain place outside the pass for several consecutive days, suggesting other intentions. Reconnaissance is currently underway. (21st Dispatch)

Tianjin, On the night of the 19th, a small number of enemies near Dongjiakou harassed our troops but were repulsed by our defending soldiers. There were no changes in the Xifengkou area as of the morning of the 21st. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, According to military sources, the enemy troops repeatedly attacked Xifengkou and subsequently Luowenyu, but were unsuccessful. Later, the enemy's fresh troops continued to arrive as reinforcements. The enemy on the front of Luowenyu has now retreated approximately fifteen li to the north to reorganize. Their subsequent troops have moved towards Languan to the west and the Jiangjunguan area, clearly intending to attack our flanks. Our forces have taken early precautions, and substantial troops have been assembled in that area, awaiting in full battle array. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

Beiping, Liu Ruming telegraphed from here on the 20th, stating that after the enemy facing Shachayu was repulsed by our troops last night, we dispatched teams to pursue and clean up the battlefield, seizing over a hundred steel helmets and countless military supplies. We also found a Manchurian map, order logs, and other items on the body of the deceased Colonel Shimamura. The enemy suffered casualties including eight officers above the rank of captain, including Captain Yoshida and Colonel Hayakawa. The enemy has now retreated to the vicinity of Banbishan. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, Song Zheyuan has returned to the front lines of Xifengkou today. According to a telegram from Xifengkou, fighting broke out there this morning, but this news has not yet been verified. (21st Reuters Dispatch)

Tang Yulin Sends Representatives to Beiping

Beiping, Tang has arrived in Boerhao, Fengning County, and is coordinating with the army. He has sent Li Shuchun to Beiping to meet with Zhu Qinglan. According to the discussions, Tang's army has been concentrated and deployed separately, and the defense lines are consolidated. On the 18th, Tang's army coordinated with the army to launch a counterattack. During a snowy night, our troops advanced over thirty li, capturing two armored vehicles, four field guns, and five machine guns. Our troops lack ammunition and supplies, and the officers and soldiers on the entire front line are burning horses for food and eating snow, unable to get enough to eat. They urgently need supplies. Tang expressed his determination to risk his remaining life to recover Chengde in order to thank the people of the country. As for the criticism from public opinion, he can only accept it without argument, hoping to make amends through future actions. (21st Dispatch)

Most Puppet Troops Lack Fighting Spirit

Beiping, According to sources from the Northeast, Zhang Haipeng's army has advanced to Chifeng. Zhang is someone who preserves his strength and is unwilling to participate in front-line combat, watching the success or failure of the Japanese. Although his unit is large, the number of personnel is insufficient, and the weapons are incomplete. It is confirmed that the puppet state has appointed Zhang Haipeng as the puppet governor of Rehe. A portion of Cheng Guorui's Second Army has been added to the front lines, while the rest remain stationed in the rear. However, the guns and personnel are not complete, the soldiers lack fighting spirit, and the opposition from the local militias and people is even more intense, with frequent and fierce clashes. (21st Dispatch)

Fierce Fighting at Jielingkou

Enemy Pummels Our Positions

Defending Troops Fight Valiantly

Enemy Troops Repulsed at Yiyuan Kou

Linyu, Over the past two days, the enemy has continuously increased its troop strength at Jielingkou, using a large amount of artillery fire and aircraft to bombard fiercely. Our officers and soldiers have fought valiantly, suffering heavy casualties, but the enemy has not been able to advance an inch. As of now, the sounds of artillery are still thundering, and fierce fighting is ongoing. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, Combined infantry, cavalry, artillery, and air units of the enemy have been fiercely attacking our Jielingkou position for days. The fighting is quite intense. On the 17th, three hundred enemy soldiers rushed in through a small path but have been surrounded by our troops. Our officers and soldiers, in coordination with a certain brigade, launched a nighttime surprise attack on the enemy's rear. The enemy could not withstand the attack and retreated in defeat. Our troops are currently pursuing them separately, while the remaining troops remain stationed at a certain location. (21st Dispatch)

Tianjin, There was fighting in the Jielingkou, Yiyuan Kou, and Taolin Kou areas on the 20th and 21st, but it was not intense. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, According to military sources, the enemy's fresh troops at Yiyuan Kou, and the surrounding passes launched particularly fierce attacks on the night of the 19th. The enemy at Yiyuan Kou have been repulsed by our certain unit. Fierce fighting is still ongoing at Jielingkou. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

Beiping, Li Yunxiang, a representative from the Relief Association, returned to Beiping from inspecting eastern . He said that Japanese and puppet troops attacked Yiyuan Kou on the 11th of this month and were met with interception by the army. After a day and night of fierce fighting, the enemy was unable to withstand the attack and withdrew from Yiyuan Kou on the afternoon of the 12th. On the 15th and 16th, Japanese troops and Zhao Lei's forces, who had defected to the enemy, attacked Yiyuan Kou again. The troops resisted bravely and fought fiercely for two days and nights, wiping out Zhao's battalion headquarters, capturing three Japanese soldiers, wounding over twenty, and seizing three enemy machine guns and over fifty rifles. are currently gathered at various passes, totaling over people, with over 6,000 guns. In addition to defending each pass and resisting the enemy, they have also organized guerrilla units to carry out guerrilla warfare. (21st Hui Dispatch)

Garrison Changeover in Luan River Area

He Zhuguo's Troops Transferred to the Rear for Rest

Japanese Aircraft Bomb Refugees on the West Bank of the Shi River, Who Move Towards Eastern Luan River Area

Tianjin, Military affairs in eastern Luan River are now under the responsibility of . The army is being transferred back to the rear for rest and replenishment. (21st Dispatch)

Tianjin, Qinhuangdao is peaceful. (21st Dispatch)

Tianjin, One enemy cruiser and two destroyers outside Dagukou left at noon on the 21st. One destroyer is still anchored. (21st Dispatch)

Tianjin, Yesterday, it was widely rumored that He Zhuguo's troops were concentrated in the Luan River area. Military authorities were asked about this, and they said that the defenses on the Luan River front were solid and that another army had been dispatched to fill the position. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, It is true that there have been troop movements in Qinhuangdao by He Zhuguo's forces. However, it is a matter of strategic necessity and not a passive retreat due to enemy pressure. There is absolutely no cause for alarm. Our troops are currently deployed very closely in certain areas, and the Qinhuangdao front remains garrisoned by our forces. All transportation continues as usual. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, Qinhuangdao Telephone Dispatch: At around 7:00 AM this morning, three Japanese aircraft bombed the area west of the Shi River, causing unknown losses. Refugees from various locations west of the Shi River are moving towards the eastern Luan River area. Japanese aircraft bombed our refugees, causing heavy casualties. There are many rumors in Qinhuangdao. (21st Dispatch)

Nanjing, According to diplomatic sources, when the fighting broke out at Yuguan, our diplomatic authorities informed the ministers and chargés d'affaires of various countries in North China that China would not be responsible for any losses suffered by the related countries if Japan were to disrupt Tianjin and Beiping. The situation in Tianjin has become tense again recently, and the government has reiterated the previous agreement. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, Xie Botan, Chief of the Military Affairs Commission's Secretariat, stated that the troop rotation in the Luan River area is a pre-planned arrangement to replenish strength and facilitate command. External rumors are not credible. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, There is no knowledge here of the report circulating in Shanghai today that Japanese authorities sent an aide-mémoire to Yu Xuezhong demanding that Chinese troops withdraw from Tianjin. (21st Reuters Dispatch)

Sun Dianying's Telegram

Destroyed Enemy Tanks

Beiping, Sun Dianying telegraphed from here on the 20th, stating that at dusk last night, the enemy facing the Liangdigoumen area used over 3,000 cavalry, over fifty tanks and armored vehicles, and a large number of infantry to launch a fierce attack on our positions, while simultaneously firing with over twenty field guns. Our troops initially remained calm, not returning fire until the tanks approached. Then, with shouts of battle, both sides engaged in close combat with broadswords and grenades. The enemy was unable to withstand the attack and retreated slightly. When our officers and soldiers were fighting to seize the tanks, the enemy inside the tanks fired machine guns and launched shrapnel and fragmentation bombs, resulting in the deaths of over ninety officers and soldiers. Finally, three tanks were destroyed, 170-180 enemies were killed, and a captured enemy company commander, Yamano Taro, will be sent to Beiping soon. Over a hundred guns were seized. As of the time of the telegram, fierce fighting was still ongoing. (21st Dispatch)

Zunhua County Magistrate's Telegram

Circumstances of Japanese Aircraft Bombing

Fires in Three Places, Ten Killed or Wounded

Public Panic and Disorder

Beiping, Liu Huanwen, the magistrate of Zunhua County, telegraphed Zhu Qinglan, stating that at noon on the 19th, five Japanese aircraft from Rehe flew to the county seat and dropped bombs, circling for over ten minutes before heading north. The people are panicking and there is great disorder. The magistrate is trying to extinguish the fires and maintain order, and has dispatched police captain Zhao Hengxin for detailed investigation. It is reported that twenty-four bombs were dropped in the county town, causing fires in three places, killing two women and three men, and wounding six people. Over ten houses were destroyed. As a result of this bombing, nine out of ten businesses have closed. It is impossible to handle all the support and relief work without funds. He urgently requests that someone be sent with a large sum of money to maintain order and facilitate military operations. Otherwise, the magistrate will be unable to maintain the situation. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, Three enemy aircraft bombed Zunhua City this morning, wounding one civilian. (21st Dispatch)

Tianjin, The Zunhua County government telegraphed the provincial government, stating that five enemy aircraft suddenly arrived at the county seat on the morning of the 20th and dropped over twenty bombs, destroying five houses and wounding over ten people, including two men and three women who were killed. (21st Dispatch)

Volunteer Army Requests Ammunition

Beiping, Zheng Guilin of the volunteer army previously sent Li to Baoding to meet with Chiang Kai-shek to discuss the allocation of ammunition and request instructions. Chiang has sent separate telegrams to the responsible authorities and garrison troops, requesting that they allocate and provide assistance nearby. Li returned to Beiping today and is scheduled to meet with He Yingqin and Zhu Qinglan tomorrow morning to discuss assistance. He will return to the front within two days. (21st Dispatch)

Japanese Military Supplies Transported to Beiping

Beiping, At 9:00 AM this morning, four iron boxcars were attached to the Beining train arriving in Beiping from Tianjin. They contained ten Japanese soldiers escorting hundreds of wooden crates of rice and military supplies. After arriving at the station, fourteen handcarts were used to transport them to the Japanese barracks in Dongjiaomin Lane. (21st Dispatch)

Three Japanese Aircraft

Bombing of Shixia Town

Enemy Troops Occasionally Harass Our Side

Beiping, Shixia Town Telephone Dispatch: At 7:00 AM this morning, three Japanese aircraft flew over and dropped over a dozen bombs, wounding three of our farmers and five soldiers. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, Over two thousand enemy troops are still stationed outside Gubeikou, Chengde, and Luanping. Strong fortifications have been built on the front line inside the pass. Apart from the five or six hundred enemy troops stationed there, the rest are puppet troops and a large number of Mongolian bandits, who occasionally harass our side. This morning, three enemy aircraft flew from the north, circling over our defense line for reconnaissance and dropping several bombs at Shixia, but they were driven away after we opened fire, causing no significant damage. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, Shixia Town Telephone Dispatch: This morning, three Japanese aircraft dropped twelve bombs, wounding four villagers. The rest fell outside the town in open areas. There were only skirmishes near the 18 Bends. The Japanese troops defending Gubeikou belong to the Nagase Detachment of the 6th Division, numbering approximately one thousand, and are equipped with fourteen heavy artillery pieces. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, According to military sources, there is an enemy supply station at Daerden, with a garrison of approximately three hundred troops. The number of enemies at Hongshan has increased to over four hundred. There are several dozen enemy infantrymen, including thirty Chinese, in Xiyu Village, fifty li from Liujiakou, reportedly scouting military information from that location to various passes. This morning, enemy aircraft reconnoitered the Nantiangmen area. The enemy at Gubeikou has increased their troop strength by approximately one company, and they are actively constructing fortifications. (21st Dispatch)

He Yingqin's Address to Troops Stationed in Nanyuan

Beiping, He Yingqin went to Nanyuan by car at 10:00 AM this morning to address the troops stationed there and returned to the Military Affairs Commission at 11:00 AM. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, Over a hundred medical soldiers from the Fifth Temporary Hospital of the Ministry of Military Administration, led by adjutant Zhang Kun, arrived here yesterday to assist with front-line medical work. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, Zhang Nanxian arrived in Beiping from Baoding this morning and then went to the Military Affairs Commission to visit He Yingqin. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, It is reported that eighty soldiers who were wounded in battles near Yanmen have recovered in various hospitals in Beiping and have now been sent back to the front lines. (21st Reuters Dispatch)

Chiang Establishes Headquarters in Beiping

Various Parties Request Government to Appoint Chiang as Commander-in-Chief

Beiping, Chiang has established headquarters in Beiping and has begun work. Huang Shaoxiong serves as the chief of staff, overseeing all matters. (21st Dispatch)

Zhenjiang, The provincial Party headquarters sent a telegram requesting the Central Government to appoint Chiang as the Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, and also requested Wang Jingwei to resume his duties. (21st Dispatch)

Beiping, The Federation of Labor Unions sent a telegram requesting the National Government to appoint Chiang as the Commander-in-Chief of the Army, Navy, and Air Force in order to achieve unified command. (21st Dispatch)

Hankou, He Chengjun arrived in Beiping on the 21st with his staff and ordered the cancellation of the Xi'an Administrative Office. The personnel of the Administrative Office, led by Zhu Huaibing, returned to Hankou. He Chengjun's mission in Beiping is to assist in all matters on the order of Chiang Kai-shek. He Chengjun sent senior staff officer Xu Chengxi to inspect the Xifengkou area. (21st Dispatch)

The Position of President of the Executive Yuan: Wang and Song Are Still Declining

Whether Wang Will Go to Baoding Is Undecided

Nanjing, Wang Jingwei underwent an examination for diabetes by his attending physician, Luo Guanghuo, on the morning of the 21st. The results showed an increase of over thirty degrees compared to when he was in Singapore, and his digestive power was also found to be weak. He immediately underwent purgative treatment. At 10:00 AM, he visited Chairman Lin again to discuss political affairs. He stated that due to his unrecovered health, he was unable to handle strenuous tasks and intended to request that Song be appointed as the substantive President of the Executive Yuan, while he would continue to serve in the Central Government, working together to deal with the national crisis. It is heard that the Central Government will discuss and decide on the 22nd whether to approve Wang's resignation as President of the Executive Yuan. As for the affairs of the Executive Yuan, Song instructed that since Wang had returned to Nanjing, he should seek Wang's instructions for handling them. Wang stated that since he had not yet resumed his duties, he should still seek Song's instructions. Therefore, the accumulated matters in the Executive Yuan must wait until next week before the Executive Yuan can convene a meeting to discuss everything. Wang Jingwei is scheduled to convene a meeting of the heads of various ministries at the official residence of the Ministry of Railways on the 22nd to discuss the policy towards Japan and his resignation as President of the Executive Yuan. (21st Dispatch)

Nanjing, Chu Minyi said that President Wang has always been extremely responsible for national affairs and is unwilling to be perfunctory. This time, he returned to the country willing to do his best to serve in the Central Government. Therefore, he only lingered in Shanghai for one day, meeting with old friends, and then hurried back to Nanjing. He is currently unable to handle strenuous tasks due to his illness. Holding the posts of Central Executive Committee member and Standing Committee member of the Central Political Council and presiding over the central government is already a heavy burden. If he were to also hold the post of President of the Executive Yuan, his illness would inevitably worsen, and outsiders might suspect that it is a political illness. Therefore, Wang still hopes that Song will be officially appointed, while he can contribute his opinions at any time. Wang's illness had not fully recovered when he returned to the country. When he was in Singapore, the sugar content tested at just over one per thousand, but the test in Shanghai increased to one hundred and forty per thousand, which has worsened. He is still continuing treatment after coming to Nanjing. The doctor advised that he must have absolute rest from 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM every day, and after blood tests, it is planned to carry out purgation within a few days to eliminate the accumulated depression in his abdomen. The date on which he will depart for Baoding to visit Chiang has not yet been determined. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

Nanjing, Peng Xuepei told reporters on the morning of the 21st that Wang plans to go north to comfort the soldiers at the front within a few days. Wang and Chiang will meet in the near future, but it has not yet been decided whether Chiang will come south or Wang will go north. Wang has not fully recovered his health and cannot resume his duties. The issue of the President of the Executive Yuan will likely be resolved in one or two days. Wang and the Central Government both prefer Song to be officially appointed, he said. (21st Dispatch)

Nanjing, President Wang went to the National Government at 9:30 AM on the 21st, then to the official residence to visit Chairman Lin for half an hour before returning to his residence. At 10:30 AM, the heads of various ministries, Chen Shaokuan, Chen Gongbo, Shi Qingyang, Chen Yi, Xu Xiqing, and Shi Ying, jointly went to visit and urged Wang to resume his duties. In the afternoon, he followed the doctor's advice and rested quietly at home. He plans to return the visits of the heads of various ministries and visit Zhang Ji, Ju Zheng, and others after 3:00 PM. (21st Dispatch)

Nanjing, Twenty-seven labor unions in Nanjing, including the industry and commerce unions, sent telegrams to the whole country, unanimously appealing to President Wang to resume his duties as soon as possible in order to strengthen the central government. (21st Dispatch)

Nanjing, The Executive Yuan meeting was held on the morning of the 21st, but Wang did not attend because he did not want to resume his duties. Currently, Wang and Song are still declining the position of President of the Executive Yuan, but all parties hope that Wang will resume his duties and are unanimously urging him. In the near future, Wang may resume his post. As for whether Wang and Chiang will meet in Baoding or Nanjing, it is still undecided. (21st Dispatch)

Nanjing, President Wang has been very busy receiving visitors since returning to Nanjing. After visiting Chairman Lin on the morning of the 21st, he rested at the mansion and had his blood tested by medical officers. In the afternoon, Central Committee members Zhang Ji, Zhu Jiahua, Shun Mengyu, Chen Gongbo, Tang Shengzhi, Zeng Zhongming, and others visited Wang's residence one after another. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

Heavy Snow and Sudden Cold in Beiping

Beiping, There is heavy snow in Beiping tonight. The ground is three to four inches deep, and the weather is extremely cold. (21st Dispatch)

Current Commentary

A View on the Future of the War of Resistance

The recent battle at Xifengkou by the troops under Song Zheyuan dealt the Japanese invaders a very significant blow. When the news of the victory arrived, the whole country rejoiced. The arrogant and powerful enemy even admitted to suffering losses of this magnitude for the first time since the Meiji Restoration's military training. The heroic, tragic, and glorious victory of this battle is worthy to be juxtaposed with the January 28th Shanghai Resistance, shining brightly in our history books. This shows that our country today is not without soldiers who are capable of enduring hardship and are willing to sacrifice their lives to fulfill their duties, nor is it without armies that can fight. It is only because of the influence of the words "non-resistance" since the September 18th Incident of the previous year that loyal and righteous people have been reduced to sighing in despair, unable to serve the country even if they wish to die for it.

Although this great victory is enough to dampen the enemy's courage and refresh international perceptions, there are still many great difficulties ahead. The victory in this battle does not mean that the enemy's aggressive steps can be stopped. What concerns us is that the anti-Japanese troops may still be fighting independently without an overall plan. We are not military experts and therefore do not know how strategy should be used. However, from the perspective of ordinary people, after this great victory by Song's troops, and with the enemy's strength greatly diminished, it would seem to be a necessary strategy to take advantage of this momentum and launch a simultaneous counterattack from all sides. However, recent war reports indicate that while fierce fighting continues at Xifengkou, other areas such as Lengkou, Gubeikou, and Shihe have entered a state of ceasefire, as if Xifengkou were engaged in a solitary struggle. For a nation invaded by others, on the verge of extinction, to have one place resisting while others watch, is like a sick person unable to flexibly use their limbs, or like a rusty machine unable to smoothly turn its wheels. This kind of independent resistance will likely be defeated by the Japanese invaders one by one. The events of January 28th serve as a recent warning.

What will happen now? Mr. Wang Jingwei said in his report at the Central Commemorative Week that "At this point, there is nothing to say except resistance." Mr. Yu Youren also said in his report at the National Government Commemorative Week, "We will never seek temporary compromise with the enemy. We would rather be shattered as jade than preserved as tile." Since the Central Government has shown such clear and firm instructions, we have no doubts. However, in view of the bloody battle of January 28th last year, which began as a lone army's struggle, followed by retreat due to being unsupported, and ended with a ceasefire and negotiation, with Shanghai returning to its life of pleasure and indulgence, we are constantly worried about repeating the mistakes of January 28th. Today's war is more important than the January 28th war. If it is unfortunate that it remains the same, then Rehe will probably never be recovered, and North China will not be able to have a day of peace. How can the people of the country not think about this?

Flying War Flags in the Sky

Opening of the German Reichstag

Hindenburg's Address Expresses Hope for Loyal Support of the Government to Restore Past Glory

Hitler's Reply States That a Fractured Germany Meant Instability for the World

Berlin - President Hindenburg and Chancellor Hitler, along with key figures from the new government, traveled by car this morning to the Potsdam Garrison Church to attend a religious ceremony marking the opening of the new Reichstag. Flags were hung and arches erected along the streets, and throngs of spectators cheered as they passed, welcoming them as conquering heroes returning in triumph. The ceremony took place at noon, and the church was extremely crowded. The former Crown Prince was also in attendance, but members of the Socialist and Communist parties were conspicuously absent. President Hindenburg delivered a solemn address, stating that the government would address the current difficult problems with unwavering resolve, and therefore its responsibility was great and complex. He hoped that the new members of the Reichstag would provide loyal support to the government. He said that those present in the church today could recall the brave, patriotic, and indomitable spirit of the former Prussians who unified the German tribes. He hoped that everyone would be inspired to work for the resurrection of a unified, free, and honorable German nation. Chancellor Hitler, in his reply, stated that after a period of prosperity, Germany had experienced economic decline, financial chaos, and millions of unemployed. Thus, the nation of poets, writers, and thinkers, driven by suffering, embraced a yearning for the rebirth of a new nation and a new life. The reforms of 1918 had come to an end, and the Kaiser and the government had what they did not want but had to do to secure Germany's freedom through battle for a new life. Germany was one of the most important elements in the world and a fractured Germany would not mean the world would be richer or happier. One notable event during today's grand ceremony was President Hindenburg's giving a Fascist-style salute to the former Crown Prince. The church was hung with old war flags, and the President raised his field marshal's baton, signaling the start of the ceremony. After delivering his address, the President placed a wreath before the tomb of Frederick the Great, then re-entered the church to pay his respects to the former Crown Prince. Shortly thereafter, he exited the church. As he left, members of the National Socialist Party all rose and gave the President a Fascist salute. The one who felt most desolate and melancholy in the church was former Chancellor Dr. Brüning, who now appeared as an insignificant figure among the members of the Reichstag. The Reichstag is scheduled to begin its work in Berlin tonight. (21st dispatch)

The Xi Government Demands Dictatorial Power

Submits Memorandum to the National Assembly

Berlin - The memorandum from the National Socialist government to the National Assembly requesting dictatorial power has now been published. It requests that the National Assembly grant the current government dictatorial power during its term in office, or until March 31, 1937. This proposal would allow the government to enact laws that conflict with the constitution and to abolish the jurisdiction of the National Assembly and the Federal Council over this legislation and over foreign treaties. (21st Reuters dispatch)

Berlin - Because the new House of Representatives is meeting in the city of Potsdam, near Berlin, thousands of tourists have arrived by train, streetcar, and bus, making it the largest crowd since 1914. The streets of Potsdam are jammed with cars, making it almost impossible to pass. The flags of the old empire, the National Socialist Party flag, and the Prussian state flag are flying everywhere. At 9:00 a.m., several units of the Reichswehr (national defense army) lined up in front of the Jesus and Catholic churches and the military garrison church. Members of the National Socialist Party and the Steel Helmet League guarded all the main roads. In front of the church steps, where Hindenburg reviewed the troops, stood many officers wearing old imperial army uniforms and steel helmets adorned with medals. The police wore peaked helmets. The crowds on the streets wore small cloth flags, either with the swastika or with the black, white, and red imperial flag, which served as emblems of the Stormtroopers (SA) and the Steel Helmet League. At 9:45 a.m., the Reichswehr honor guard arrived in Potsdam, led by a military band and carrying military flags, and took their position next to the military garrison church. Because of the large crowds, the landlords of the houses facing the military garrison church rented out their balconies for viewing, with rental prices reaching 2,000 francs. The police maintained strict security, with police officers stationed on the rooftops. (21st Havas dispatch)

Key to European Stability

France Does Not Object to Joining the European Four-Power Pact

British and French Prime Ministers Meet Again

Careful Consultation on Details of Agreement

London - According to the latest news from Paris today, the talks between the British and Italian Prime Ministers in Rome have indeed shown signs of improving the European situation. According to news from Paris, there is now a possibility of rapprochement between France and Italy. It is reported that French Prime Minister Daladier and Foreign Minister Flandin, after consulting with their cabinet members tonight, will inform their British counterparts at tomorrow's meeting that the French government is willing to support the British authorities' work in Rome. It is widely believed that the talks over the past few days will have a significant positive impact on diplomatic relations among European countries, and the repeated declarations of no recourse to arms will have a very pleasant psychological effect, helping to restore public confidence. According to informed sources, France is prepared to participate in a pact of a consultative nature, but France must have sufficient time to study the details. (20th Reuters dispatch)

Paris - British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon arrived here this morning from Rome. Prime Minister Daladier and Foreign Minister Flandin welcomed them at the station, and the British delegation immediately traveled by car to the British Embassy. (21st National Telegram)

British and French Prime Ministers

Consult on Terms of Agreement

Paris - The main objective of the agreement drafted by the British and Italian authorities in Rome is to promote ten years of cooperation in Europe in the spirit of the non-aggression pact. This agreement could be extended to overseas colonies in the future. The agreement stipulates that the peace treaties will be revised in accordance with the provisions of the League of Nations Covenant. Britain, France, and Italy agree to recognize Germany's equal rights and allow Germany to reorganize its army to have the same status as other European countries. Austria, Hungary, and Bulgaria will be given the same treatment. The agreement will last for ten years, and if no notice of termination is given one year in advance, it will continue for another ten years. British and French prime ministers and diplomatic officials met at the British Embassy this morning to discuss the terms of the Anglo-Italian agreement. Although the French government has neither acknowledged nor denied the aforementioned terms, semi-official sources believe that some terms still need to be revised and subjected to very careful study. The French media believes that this agreement could bring about major changes in Europe. (21st Reuters dispatch)

Reported by British Newspapers

Outline of Draft Pact

Paris - The outline of Mussolini's new peace pact, as reported by the London Daily Telegraph, has today received semi-official confirmation here. It is said that the draft guarantees cooperation between Britain, Italy, France, and Germany to maintain peace in Europe. Other countries may also join, provided they formally ratify the new pact. However, after the ten-year term of the new pact, these joining countries will have no right to terminate or extend the pact. The four countries also recognize that Germany should have equal rights to armaments, and the time has come to implement this principle of equality. In order to ensure that the new pact is fully effective, France, Britain, and Italy must find ways to revise the various peace treaties. The League of Nations Covenant already contains such provisions, and the same will now be done for Austria and Bulgaria. In addition, it is reported that the draft also stipulates that the countries concerned will attempt to implement these provisions outside of Europe and in matters relating to colonial affairs. (21st National Telegram)

Key to Success or Failure

Hangs on Paris Talks

Rome - The acceptance by British Prime Minister MacDonald of Mussolini's plan is generally welcomed here, and is seen as a major victory for Mussolini. However, the pact of a consultative nature among the four powers is still in its embryonic stage, and success or failure depends on whether France agrees to cooperate with Britain and Italy to stabilize peace in Europe. The current obstacle to cooperation is the discord between France and Italy, which stems from the Italian belief that Italy did not receive what it deserved in the Great War, and from France's assistance to Yugoslavia and its refusal to grant Italy naval equality with France. As for the relationship between France and Germany, Italy is capable of persuading German Chancellor Hitler, and the British Prime Minister is capable of persuading France, so that is not a cause for concern. (21st Reuters dispatch)

Washington - British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon will be discussing the plan proposed by the Italian Prime Minister with French officials in Paris tomorrow. People here regard the Anglo-French talks as very important, because Italy has stated that Mussolini's plan is not limited to the four major powers, and British Prime Minister MacDonald is very concerned about the future attitude of Poland and the Little Entente countries. Therefore, it is generally believed that the key to the issue lies in the meeting in Paris. (20th Havas dispatch)

French Newspapers Fear

Losing Their Leading Position

Paris - French newspapers are still engaged in criticizing the Italian Prime Minister's plan, saying that while the Franco-British talks are important, it is difficult to achieve results with this plan. They also stated that France does not want to abandon Italy's suggestions, but the Rome conference and today's talks between the British and French authorities here will be a prelude to lengthy negotiations. As for France's views, the semi-official Temps summarized them by saying that a new idea has entered the situation at the end of this week, but no one knows to what extent it will develop. (21st National Telegram)

Paris - The French media maintains a lukewarm attitude towards the four-power peace pact recently proposed by Mussolini, and unanimously rejects it as untimely. French newspapers have put forward two major reasons, saying that the establishment of a peace treaty between the four major powers would be a great loss to the various small countries, and that France would lose its significant influence in European politics. Le Matin claims that if France joins the four-power pact, the various small countries will cease their enthusiasm for supporting France, which would be tantamount to actually reducing France's military strength. Therefore, since France has reduced its military strength and been deprived of the support of its allies, it will henceforth be subject to the will of its powerful neighbors and will have to make concessions again and again. (21st National News Agency dispatch)

German Public Opinion

Sympathetic to the Italian Prime Minister's Plan

Berlin - It is not known here what the real significance is of the plan proposed by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, so German public opinion is reserving judgment. However, it is said that the plan for cooperation among the four powers did not begin today. Berlin has advocated it before, but no one agreed to it. However, the Italian Prime Minister's plan includes the revision of certain provisions of the peace treaty and the implementation of the principle of equality in armaments. German public opinion expresses considerable sympathy for the Italian Prime Minister on this point. (20th Havas dispatch)

The American Side

Concerned About the Situation in Europe

Washington - The plan proposed by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has attracted great attention in political and journalistic circles. However, the State Department is maintaining silence. The State Department is well aware of the difficulty of bringing French and German views closer together. The Italian Prime Minister's plan may be seen as capable of restoring peace in Europe. President Roosevelt believes that the recovery of American industry and commerce depends on the success of the disarmament conference and the world economic conference. Even partial success would be beneficial. Therefore, Roosevelt is extremely concerned about the situation in Europe. The American disarmament representative, Davis, will probably meet with French Foreign Minister Flandin. (20th Havas dispatch)

The Little Entente Countries

Deeply Fear Being Sidelined

Capital of Yugoslavia - Political figures here are quite worried that the four-power committee plan proposed by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will sideline the Balkan Little Entente countries (i.e., Yugoslavia, Romania, and Czechoslovakia), and they believe that this policy may bankrupt the various organs of the League of Nations. (20th Havas dispatch)

Japanese Army Convenes

Division Commanders' Conference

Actively Improve National Armaments

Tokyo - After the regular reshuffle of the army, the army will convene a division commanders' conference for five days starting on the 28th. Orders to attend the conference have been sent to Abe, the commander of the Taiwan Army, Kawashima, the commander of the Korean Army, the division commanders of each division, and the commanders of the reserve divisions. The agenda for the conference is as follows: (28th) Audience with the Emperor, commanders of each army and division commanders report on the military situation, followed by a meal with the Emperor. (29th) The Minister of the Army delivers an address at the Ministry of the Army, followed by a meeting. (30th) Prince Kan'in, the Chief of the General Staff, delivers an address at the General Staff Headquarters, followed by a continuation of the meeting. (31st) The Director-General of Military Education, General Hayashi, delivers an address, followed by a continuation of the meeting. (April 1st) Hunting. (21st Den-tsu dispatch)

Tokyo - Since the budget for improving the army's armaments has been approved, the Ministry of the Army has begun to work on fully staffing the army, implementing supplementary education, and preparing operational materials. The main content is as follows: 1. Improve equipment and increase new elite units. The necessary personnel will be gradually summoned from among reserve officers and non-commissioned officers for emergency training. 2. Increase the summoning and implementation of reserve second and first lieutenants and warrant officers as a transitional measure. 3. Increase the number of students entering military academies and juvenile schools. 4. Establish a non-commissioned officer institution to train special forces. 5. Establish a new educational institution for defense against poison gas. (21st Den-tsu dispatch)

Hong Kong - Rong Zhongwei, a member of the Fourth Air Squadron of Guangdong, crashed his plane at Slim Dog Ridge this morning while flying, and died. The plane was destroyed. (21st Special Dispatch)

Wu Qiwel Captures Guangchang

Bandits Fleeing to Nanxiong

After several days of stalemate, Datian City was captured on the 13th and the bandits retreated to Jianning. The Bandit 5th Division of more than 3,000 people in the Ganbian area attempted to attack Jianyang. Many bandits disguised as beggars were sent to spy. The Bandit 7th and 8th Divisions in Fangshao are wandering northwest of Chong'an and are being encircled and suppressed separately. (21st Special Dispatch)

Nanchang - Chiang designated Nanchang as the rear defense after the suppression of the Communists and appointed the brigade commander as the commander of the urban area. (21st Special Dispatch)

Han Fuju Returns to Jinan

Delivers Speech to Various Circles in Dezhou

Jinan - Han Fuju, accompanied by Ge Guangting, Zhang Yue, Zhang Liansheng, Yao Yijia, and others, arrived in Jinan by special train at 9:00 p.m. Leaders from the party, government, and military circles greeted them at the station. Han said that the impression of this trip was very good and that the Commander-in-Chief was determined to resist. Everything in front is now arranged very closely by Minister He. All the generals and soldiers are determined to resist. They are now digging deep trenches and building high fortresses to wait. The fighting at Xifengkou and Gubeikou is going well. He was ordered to return quickly to prepare everything in order and maintain the security of the province. He had the honor of meeting with the Commander-in-Chief twice, but there was no time to discuss politics. Ge said that he was ordered to go to Baoding and did not have any special mission. He will return to Qingdao tonight. Han also said that he had the honor of meeting Minister He Wanfulin and others twice in Peiping. Liu Xizhong stayed in Peiping. (21st Special Dispatch)

Jinan - Han convened a meeting of military, government, and civilian representatives in Dezhou Pingyuan today. There was a heavy snowstorm at the time, but several thousand people attended. Before the speech, everyone sang the battle action song. The main points of the speech were to elaborate on the tragic situation of Vietnam and Korea being subjugated, and to hope that all circles would work hard to fight. International warfare requires the total mobilization of the entire population and cannot rely solely on the military. (21st Special Dispatch)

Tianjin - Han Fuju's special train arrived in Tianjin at 8:00 a.m. on the 21st and went to the provincial government for breakfast. He left Tianjin at 9:30 a.m. to return to Jinan. (21st Special Dispatch)

Song Zheyuan Replies to Zhang Zhijiang by Telegram

My brother has always held the determination to fight to the death against the enemy. I would be very happy if we could share the hardships together and defend the territory." Zhang replied to Song again, saying, "Our army has been winning battles for days, shaking the world. I am both pleased and angry. I am far away and thinking of all my comrades fighting the enemy, but using bayonets and hot blood to resist the enemy's new weapons. These heroic actions have moved even women and children, let alone my brother, who has always shared weal and woe with you and wants to bravely come forward. But I am being held back by matters and my spirit is with you day and night. I telegraphed Chiang on the 14th, asking for an assignment, but have not received a reply. If I can get permission, I will personally see my brothers achieve the victory of destroying the enemy and sweeping away their lairs. At 2:00 p.m., they captured Nanjiang City. The bandits fled in droves to Dazhai and Xiaozhai. They are currently continuing the pursuit. Before leaving, the bandits dragged away all men and women under the age of 40 and massacred more than 1,000 civilians, which was extremely brutal. (20th Special Dispatch)

Liu Shouzhong Requests Resignation as Supervisory Commissioner

Nanjing: Liu Shouzhong, deeply concerned about the daily deepening foreign aggression and determined to resist the invaders, has specially telegraphed Chairman Lin and President Yuan, earnestly requesting to resign from his position as Supervisory Commissioner of Shaanxi and Shanxi provinces, requesting the appointment of other capable individuals to avoid delaying important matters, and has also telegraphed Zhang Ji, requesting him to convey his firm intention so that he can dedicate his efforts to the border regions. Discussions about the advancement and retreat of administrative officials versus political officials are a political malpractice in our country, and he deeply hopes to eradicate this practice from the national personnel agency. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 21st)

Negotiations Regarding Water Pipes in the Capital City

Nanjing: During Wei Daoming's tenure, water pipes for the capital were ordered from the French company Paris Factory. Contracts were signed for delivery and payment, stipulating deadlines. The goods were not delivered in full, but the payment was already made, which deviated from the original intention of the contract. The original specified thickness of the manufactured water pipes was 45 millimeters, but upon delivery, they were only 13 millimeters, resulting in bursts. Shi Ying has repeatedly negotiated with the Paris Factory, insisting on compensation for the burst water pipes and guarantees that the French company will bear all losses for any bursts within two years. The French company has sent personnel to Nanjing to negotiate. Our side must achieve the goals of compensation and guarantees; otherwise, the water pipe bursts will be announced to the world. U.S. Congress to

Discuss Silver Issue Next Month

No Additional Taxes on Silver for Commercial Use

Washington Dispatch, 20th of the Republic: Senator Pittman stated today after accompanying Congressional Democratic leaders to a meeting at the White House, "The issues of reminting silver coins and stabilizing silver prices will be considered after Congress concludes the current emergency session." It is understood that the silver issue was discussed at length during this White House meeting. This meeting took place after the U.S. Bureau of Mines released world silver production statistics, which indicated a total of 11,674,000 ounces in January, the highest record since November 1931, due to a surge in production from Mexican silver mines. President Timothy immediately summoned Senate leaders to discuss this matter. It is reported that Pittman presented detailed opinions, requesting the government to purchase silver in the world market to sufficiently increase silver prices, and stated that silver subsidiary coins should be reminted to allow the U.S. to increase trade with South America and China. None of the attendees expressed the President's attitude. However, judging from Pittman's statement, it is evident that Roosevelt will at least be willing to

Allow the silver issue to be debated in Congress. Currently, there are four proposals regarding the silver issue: one, Senator Dill's proposal to purchase silver and issue new banknotes; two, Senator Wheeler's proposal to remint silver coins at a ratio of sixteen to one; three, Senator Pittman's proposal to purchase silver; and four, an amendment to the Glass-Steagall Banking Act to reduce the pure gold content in gold dollars. All four proposals were explained in detail to the President today. The Congressional session is expected to open around the end of April.

Reuters Washington Dispatch, 20th: U.S. Treasury Secretary Woodin stated on March 16th that silver used in commercial exchanges would not be subject to restrictions, but restrictions would be imposed on those attempting to hoard it. It has been learned that Woodin's statement refers to the regulations issued under the authority granted to the Secretary by President Roosevelt's declarations of March 5th and March 9th. It is reported that legitimate silver transactions will not be restricted, but if depositors withdraw large amounts of cash with the intention of storing them abroad, such withdrawals will be prohibited upon confirmation.

Former Commander-in-Chief of British Navy in China Dies

Reuters London Dispatch, 20th: Admiral Sir Jerram, who served as Commander-in-Chief of the British Navy in China from 1913 to 1915, passed away today at the age of 75. He commanded the 2nd Battle Squadron during the Battle of Jutland in World War I and was promoted to Admiral in 1917.

Japan Resolves to Sever Ties with the League of Nations

Withdrawal Procedures Document Divided into Four Sections

Statement and Accompanying Documents More Important

Still Dreaming of Cooperation Between China, Japan, and Manchukuo

Formal Notification Delayed Again and Again

Habe Issues Statement to Reassure the Public

China League Agency Tokyo Correspondence: Japan's consultation on withdrawing from the League of Nations is still under consideration by the Privy Council. The procedures are scheduled to be submitted on the 27th, divided into (Notification of Withdrawal from the League of Nations), (Statement), (Accompanying Documents), and reference materials, totaling over 2,000 pages. Among them, the statement and accompanying documents are more important as they outline Japan's policies. An abridged translation is as follows:

Key Points of the Statement

1. Restate the process of withdrawing from the League, praising cooperation during its membership, and then state the purpose of withdrawing from the League, which is to carry out Japan's Far Eastern policy. 2. Although Japan is withdrawing from the League of Nations, it will continue to uphold international peace and cooperate with all countries in the world, working to promote world peace and enhance human happiness. 3. In the future, Japan will participate in disarmament conferences convened by the League of Nations or peaceful endeavors aimed at economic or cultural facilities as a non-League member, providing effective and appropriate cooperation. 4. Regarding maintaining peace in the Far East, Japan is determined to assume its responsibility, but is willing to cooperate with countries with interests in China. 5. With the belief of recognizing its independence, provide benevolent assistance to (Manchukuo) and support it to the end. 6. The policy towards China is to quickly restore proper friendly relations, expecting China to become a completely independent country as soon as possible. Therefore, providing assistance for internal affairs and the necessary friendly assistance. During this period, make China recognize (Manchukuo) independence as an accomplished fact, hoping that the relationship between China, Japan, and Manchukuo can be resolved peacefully.

The matters described in the accompanying documents are related to the follow-up measures after withdrawing from the League of Nations. Excerpts of its content are as follows: First, after withdrawing from the League, Japan still has the right to participate in the General Assembly and Administrative Council of the League for the next two years in terms of law. Since the actual participants are few, the Japanese government has decided not to participate in the meeting. Second, the expenses to be borne by the Japanese government after withdrawing from the League of Nations will be calculated on a daily basis and paid off, fulfilling its obligations. Third, Japanese staff serving in the League of Nations do not have to

Accompanying Documents

Retreat together with the government. For those who voluntarily resign, the government will find ways to arrange or assist them. Fourth, the following measures are prescribed for the handling of various League of Nations agencies after withdrawal: 1. Deal with China, Russia, and European and American countries with covert tactics, avoiding causing trouble and creating incidents, thereby removing the anxiety of China and foreign countries. 2. Continue to cooperate with various specialized agencies affiliated with the League of Nations, showing Japan's impartiality. If it is beneficial to Japan, the League of Nations General Assembly and Administrative Council have political colors, so they will not participate. Other peaceful undertakings, administrative contacts, etc. should still continue to cooperate. However, if there are any agencies that are detrimental to Japan, cooperation will be canceled at any time. 3. Continue to cooperate with various agencies established under treaties, such as the Mandates Commission, the International Office of Public Health, the International Air Navigation Commission, the International Hydrographic Bureau, the Straits Commission, the General Transport Council, and the Central Opium Board. 4. The International Economic and Financial Conference is closely related to Japan. Participation is beneficial. After Japan withdraws from the League, Ambassador Ochiai and Finance Officer Tsushima will still participate in the meeting. 5. The articles of the International Labor Organization are inserted in the 13th part of the Treaty of Peace with Germany and are somewhat different in nature from the League of Nations. The International League has many political colors, while the International Labor Organization is still a social and humanitarian organization, and has a very large autonomy over the League of Nations. Not only should it not be cut off, but it should cooperate with this organization, and cooperation is considered a wise way to ensure peace. When Brazil and Spain left the League of Nations, they also declared cooperation with the International Labor Organization, which was caused by recognizing the special nature of this organization.

China League Tokyo Electric Dispatch, 20th: Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations has been delayed again and again. It was said on the 24th that it was too late, and it was said that the procedures would be submitted on the 27th. The Japanese people deeply believe that the Japanese government cannot quickly decide because it is secretly expecting Britain and France to serve as mediators. However, Britain and France are still as quiet as Mount Tai, with no intention of intervening. News of this has generated various rumors within the country, and people's hearts are shaking. From anxiety to pessimism, and then to self-abandonment, the Japanese Navy is very worried that it will not fall to the outside but to the inside. Today, a statement was issued in the form of a conversation with a senior official to reassure the public. Its words are: (The world will never blockade Japan because Japan withdrew from the League of Nations. If Japan is really blocked, the navy will immediately blockade Chinese ports, cutting off all countries' trade with China. Japan will use strong trade to maintain its economy during times of crisis, and the losers will be Britain, France, the United States, Italy, and other countries. The countries are too busy to take care of themselves and will never dare to cause a second world war with a blockade policy. Therefore, there is no economic blockade, and there is no world war. The Japanese Navy has insufficient power to attack the world, but it has more than enough power to retreat and defend Asian territories. If the League of Nations or the United States interfere with the South Pacific Islands, we will deal with them with strength. Please do not worry too much), etc.

Disarmament Conference

Will Enter a New Stage

The General Committee Will Reopen Tomorrow

British Plan to Be Discussed

Havas, Geneva Dispatch, 20th: The British government still wants the disarmament conference to start a general discussion of the British disarmament plan starting from Thursday. Foreign Minister Simon will arrive here soon. It is generally believed that Simon will ask the General Committee to discuss the British proposal in a special procedure. The British delegation does not want the British proposal to be scattered in the hands of multiple committees, so it will firmly request that the General Committee be solely responsible for item-by-item discussions. The British delegation also wants the governments of various countries to express their opinions on each item within a short period of time. The British are eager for the disarmament conference to express itself quickly, and its psychology is easy to understand. However, it is doubtful whether the governments of various countries can satisfy Britain's wishes less than a week after the British plan was proposed. Most delegations have not only not sought the opinions of their respective national defense agencies, but also the representatives have not studied the issues raised by the British plan in detail from a political point of view. In this situation, it would be too hasty to ask them to express their opinions on the British proposal immediately. Therefore, the meeting of the General Committee on Thursday will still not exceed the scope of general discussion. Major countries will definitely want to judge the British plan in its entirety, especially the secondary countries that have not expressed their opinions at the meeting on Friday. However, governments will never want to express definite views before soliciting the necessary opinions. But in any case, the disarmament conference will enter a new active stage after Thursday.

On New Disarmament Plan

Japan Opposes the Following Points

Reuters Tokyo Dispatch, 21st: Japan does not approve of the British Prime Minister's disarmament plan. Japan requests that Japan's suggestions be discussed together.
