Free Talk

"Where Light Arrives..."

— He Jiagan

Torture in Chinese prisons is an open secret. Last month, the China League for Civil Rights brought up this issue.

But the foreign-run (North-China Daily News) published a (Beijing Dispatch) on February 15, detailing that Dr. Hu Shih had personally visited several prisons and (very affectionately) told this reporter that (according to his careful investigation, he could not obtain the slightest evidence that they could easily talk to the prisoners. Once, Dr. Hu Shih was even able to converse with them in English. The prison conditions, he (Dr. Hu Shih - Jiagan's note) said, were not satisfactory, but although they freely (oh, very freely! - Jiagan's note) complained about the poor treatment and insults, they did not even hint at torture.)

Although I did not have the honor of following this (careful investigation), I visited the Beijing Model Prison ten years ago. Although it was a model prison, visiting prisoners and talking was not very (free). There was a window in between, about three feet apart. A guard stood next to me, the time was limited, and talking in code was not allowed, let alone in a foreign language.

But this time, Dr. Hu Shih was (able to converse with them in English,) which is extremely special. Could it be that Chinese prisons have been improved to this extent, (free) to this extent? Or was the guard intimidated by (English), thinking that Dr. Hu Shih was a fellow countryman of Lord Lytton and had a great background?

Fortunately, I saw Dr. Hu Shih's inscription on the (China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Three Major Cases)!

(Public exposure is the only weapon to overthrow dark politics. Where light arrives, darkness disappears.) (There were no modern punctuation marks originally; I added these presumptuously - Jiagan's note.)

I was thus greatly enlightened. It is not allowed to converse with prisoners in foreign languages in prisons, but Dr. Hu Shih opened a special case as soon as he arrived because he can (publicly expose), he can talk (very affectionately) with foreigners, he is (light), so (where light arrives, darkness) (disappears). He then (publicly exposed) the China League for Civil Rights to foreigners, and (darkness) fell on this side. But I wonder if this (light) will allow others to converse with prisoners in (English) forever after returning to his residence?

If it is not allowed, then it is (light leaves, and darkness returns).

And this (light) is also busy with the affairs of the Boxer Indemnity Committee and cannot often go into (darkness). Before the second (careful investigation) of the prison, the prisoners probably will not have the (very free) happiness of speaking (English) again. Alas, light only follows (light), and the world of light in prison is truly very temporary!

However, this cannot be blamed on anyone. They should never have committed a (crime). (Good people) will never commit a (crime). If you don't believe it, look at this (light)!

Barbusse Comes to China

— Zheng Boqi

At a time when Jehol has fallen, Tianjin and Beijing are in danger, and imperialism is intensifying its conspiracy to partition China, Barbusse, an (anti-imperialist) writer, has been entrusted by the (Anti-Imperialist League) to come to China with other committee members to conduct an on-the-spot investigation of the truth of Japanese imperialism's aggression against China. This is something that Chinese writers, and even people who love literature, should pay attention to.

Since the (September 18th) Incident, Japan has expanded the war without hindrance. The United States' observation, the League of Nations' mediation, and the elusive attitude of Britain and France all fully expose the united front of imperialism against China. The working masses have long felt the absolute opposition between imperialism and the Chinese national independence movement. In the sound of the Japanese cannons, a huge anti-imperialist movement has been launched on the East Asian continent.

The imperialist international, in order to maintain its prestige and to realize the conspiracy to partition China, sent Lytton and seven other military personnel and politicians to China to investigate through the League of Nations. The report of this international investigation team did not advocate for Japan to withdraw its troops, but only nakedly depicted the plan and steps for partitioning China. Except for the higher-ups among the Chinese, such as Hu Shih, everyone expressed their firm opposition. However, the imperialist powers did not relax their plan to partition China because of this. Now that Jehol has fallen and Tianjin and Beijing are in danger, the emperor emeritus of the East Legation Quarter is secretly active again. The people of the whole country are worried, anxious, and indignant, and Barbusse and others are coming to China!

The task of Barbusse and his entourage in coming to China is the same as that of the League of Nations investigation team led by Lytton, to investigate the various atrocities of Japanese imperialism since the (September 18th) Incident. However, their position is completely different. They are against imperialism, and they will never hide anything for violent Japan. They are against imperialism, and they will never advocate the poisonous plan of partitioning or jointly managing China. No, even further, they are as firmly opposed to partitioning and joint management as we are. They are against imperialism, and they will definitely support our anti-imperialist upsurge.

From this point of view, Barbusse and his entourage are completely our friends. Shouldn't we express our welcome?

Random Notes from Qulu

— Zizhan

The English word "Humour" is translated as "幽默" (youmo - humorous) , which began with Lin Yutang. Today, these two characters are used together as a word and are commonly understood by scholars, just as "Utopia" is translated as "乌托邦" (wutuobang - utopia), and "Modern" is translated as "摩登" (modeng - modern) by Tian Han. Mr. Lin recently edited the "Analects Half-Monthly" and used "humor" as a call to action. Mr. Li Qingya believes that translating "humor" as "语妙" (yumiao - witty words) is better, as it can take into account both sound and meaning. Mr. Chen Wangdao wants to translate it as the "油滑" (youhua - slick) of "油腔滑调" (youqianghuadiao - glib talk). The speaker is serious, and the listeners laugh. Someone said that the Russian word equivalent to humor is translated as "狗不咬" (goubuyao - dog doesn't bite), which is simply laughable. I have recently seen that so-called humorous articles mostly take subtle sarcasm as their forte, just like what Mr. Yi Yincun calls "特别优骂" (tebie youma - especially elegant scolding). He wants to replace "humor" with "优骂" (youma - elegant scolding). However, the word "humor" is popular and unimpeded. As Xunzi said, "What is agreed upon by custom is called appropriate," so I have not yet openly proposed "优骂" as a term for discussion to Messrs. Chen, Li, and Lin. While ill, I flipped through "Gutong Miscellaneous Notes" in the "Jia Yin Weekly." Mr. Gutong does not think it is right for the word "humor" to be misunderstood. He roughly said that the word "humor" seems to be translated from the English "Humour," which refers to the wit of those who are good at making witty remarks, but the literal meaning is slightly contrary, which easily leads to misunderstandings. The sentiment of writing is always obtained between the lines, which is called "everything is in the unspoken words." However, the unspoken words are the unspoken words in the spoken words. If there are no words from the beginning, how can we know the difference between words and silence being just right. People in the Tang Dynasty liked to make allegorical sayings, thinking it was interesting, but without the former, there is no way to see the latter. If not a word is spoken, how can the wonderfulness of reality and illusion be known. I once argued that transliteration is the best method for protecting nouns, but if the meaning of Chinese characters is mixed in, so that both sound and meaning can be taken care of, one may accidentally end up with words as ugly as "ice unicorn." Although the drawbacks of the word "humor" are not to this extent, frequent misuse is very bad. How about replacing it with the characters "酉靺"? Mr. Gutong's argument was published eight years ago, and few people paid attention to it at the time. Now, the word "humor" has become a common word in the mouths of new people. Movie advertisements and cosmetics advertisements also want to borrow the word "humor" to attract attention.

(Pretty Boys) and Their (Culture)

— Xingzhi

(1)

Whenever someone mentions (pretty boys), everyone immediately can visualize a (face like powder, lips like rouge, eyes full of emotion, words like laughter, naturally charming, all in the eyebrows, a lifetime of thoughts, all in the corners of the eyes) handsome young man. Jia Baoyu is a pretty boy, Tang Bohu is also a pretty boy. Throughout history, there are as many pretty boys as the countless sands of the Ganges.

Jia Baoyu once said: (Men are made of mud). Because they are made of mud, they melt into a mess as soon as they see (women made of water). The (men) that Jia Dashao is talking about here, of course, only refer to (pretty boys) like himself. This means that the highest authority of pretty boys is (women), and even the will to live of pretty boys is nothing but (women). Taking women as the driving force of life and women as the source of life, they are happy to do everything that can please women. Therefore, our Jia Dashao would lick the rouge on women's faces, accompany Lin Meimei to cry, be full of illnesses, be sentimental, be foolish, and also write poetry and lyrics, play drinking games, and gamble... Because (beauties) love (talented men), it has been like this since ancient times, so most pretty boys are also (talented men). Jia Baoyu and Tang Bohu are two examples.

Now, pretty boys are naturally still the same (face like powder, lips like rouge) pretty boys as before, but the times are advancing after all, and pretty boys are of course also advancing. What are they advancing in? Playing mahjong, dancing Charleston, singing "Sister, I Love You," filling in liberation lyrics. Occasionally, if they can't fill them in, they steal a poem or two from the ancients (and still insist that it rhymes with the original). They can also brag, flatter, and fabricate rumors. There is also a bit of progress, which is that pretty boys in ancient times, like Jia Baoyu, mostly despised fame and wealth, while today's pretty boys can use bragging and flattery to get some nominal positions in some departments or associations and receive unearned salaries.

In short, (pretty boys) are made of mud, are the most sentimental, are weak and unable to withstand the wind, only know how to drink alcohol, play mahjong, write nauseating poems and lyrics, write several bundles of love letters and something like essays. They have no will, no life, no vitality, and even no bones. They cannot stand or sit still, and can only lean on (pillows) and linger in sorrow. National affairs (damn it), everything (damn it). Although they sometimes complain, it is only (complaining) in the end. This is (pretty boys), a ghost, a living corpse.

(2)

So, what is (pretty boy culture)?

That is the History of Swirling Palaces, "Sister, I Love You," the Charleston dance, passion, love, infatuation, sorrow, tears, wine, thighs, cherry lips, spring's fallen flowers, autumn's red leaves, loneliness, desolation, melancholy, complaints, "My love, my heart, my darling," the tragic cries of ghosts, the groans of the ill, the chirping of dying autumn insects. In short, it is disillusionment, decline, and escape from reality.

(3)

A ghost, a living corpse, what does this era need them for? Decline, you (declining class)'s groaning! Decline, your declining class's culture!

Editor's Note: Recently, several gentlemen, in view of the new literary world being gloomy and ghostly figures walking around in broad daylight, volunteered to write articles to reprimand two or three petty thieves. In order to maintain the literary world and eliminate literary demons, this journal is happy to publish such critical articles that (benefit the world and people's hearts). In recent days, we have received letters from all parties praising us, which shows that (justice is in people's hearts). However, due to the limited space in this journal and the fact that there are more important tasks waiting to be started, this type of criticism will be temporarily terminated from today.

Full-Length Creative Work

Crossroads of Era and Love

— Zhang Guanping

(I am your fellow villager, surnamed Lin.)

Before Haiquan could finish speaking, the door opened. He saw Madam Cao wearing a deep blue patterned cotton cheongsam, which was even more unsightly than when he saw her at the church that day. But her face was still covered with white powder. Only those rows of pearly teeth were very moving. She opened her clothes, revealing a nipple, and was breastfeeding her child. Haiquan saw her breasts, which were also white and somewhat moving.

(Oh, Mr. Lin? I'm sorry, I thought it was someone else. Ha, ha, ha, please come in and sit.

Seeing Madam Cao's generous attitude, Haiquan felt a sense of pressure and didn't know how to deal with her.

(Where is Lao Cao?)

(He went out and will be back in a moment. Sit down. Please wait a moment, he will be back.)

Haiquan had no choice but to follow her in. He saw that their room had a bed, a small desk, a small round table, two wooden chairs, and four round wooden stools - the stool surfaces were painted with vulgar black lacquer orchids. These pieces of furniture and the furnishings on the table were all cluttered and disorganized. From this, it was not difficult to see the daily life of the couple. After Haiquan sat down on a chair, he still smelled a stench of urine. He then saw a large pile of wet diapers piled up in the corner of the bed, which were dirty and black.

Madam Cao put down the child in her arms, still exposing her nipple, poured a cup of slightly cloudy tea that looked like ox urine, and smiled as she handed it to Haiquan. He always felt that her smile was not very generous.

Haiquan was lost in thought for a moment and inadvertently noticed a very beautiful stroller in the corner of the door in front of him.

(That's a beautiful stroller, it must not be cheap!)

He asked with a smile.

(It's not necessarily that good, but in any case, we can't afford it. It was a gift from Lao Ha when the child turned one month old). (Lao Ha is being too kind.)

(What does that count for! To them Americans, dozens of dollars is not the same as a few dimes to us.)

The child started crying on the bed.

(So annoying! I have to hold it every minute! It really prevents me from taking a single step. I really want to throw you into the Huangpu River before I'm satisfied!)

Madam Cao deliberately said with gritted teeth and exaggeratedly. But she still went over and picked up the child. She showed her breasts even more unceremoniously.

(Where did Lao Cao go? Is he at Lao Ha's place again?)

(Isn't he!)

At this time, she gave Haiquan an unnatural flirtatious smile for no reason. Haiquan saw it and felt a slight chill. He wondered what this meant. He felt that this room was as cold as the Crystal Palace, no wonder the child's philtrum was covered with grayish-white snot.

(Did he have to go so early? Didn't he say that he usually goes in the afternoon?)

(There is something special today.)

(What is it?)

Commercial News

Finance

The Inevitable Stage After a Sharp Rise

The Gold Standard Turns Towards Reactionary Advances

Abundant Elasticity Creates a Triangular Process

Appearing at $1086, Ultimately Falling a Strong $13

Although the gold market opened low yesterday, the upward trend in the middle was not weak, reaching a new high price of $1086 (after the abolition of taels and the adoption of the yuan). However, due to unfavorable market sentiment, many people sold off, trending downwards. As a result, the closing price was lower than the previous day's. In the early morning, London telegraphic transfers (T/T) for both near and far terms decreased by 1.25, the New York silver price only fell by 1.25, the British-American exchange rate was down by 0.0225, the American-British exchange rate was also down by 0.0175, the forward price fell by 3 to 5 percent, and American cotton remained largely unchanged. All these factors failed to satisfy people. Bank private telegrams also only fell by 1.25. Due to unfavorable market sentiment, the opening price immediately dropped to $1074.5. The exchange market opened flat but slightly firm, with the British exchange rate at 1 shilling 8.125 pence and the American exchange rate at $28.875. Initially, it was extremely flat; American exchange rates for April at $29.125, May at $29.375, and June at $29.75 could all be settled. Subsequently, it retreated to around $29.70. Afterwards, it gradually improved. Jardine Matheson and Mitsui both offered June American dollars at $29.75. Buying interest gradually intensified, but when the June American exchange rate reached $29.625 and could not be settled, it broke through to beyond $29.80. Furthermore, because the June American exchange rate at $29.50 was difficult to settle, coupled with the announcement of the HSBC exchange rate, the shilling remained unchanged, and the American exchange rate further decreased by 1.25, adding fuel to the fire and surging to $1086. However, thereafter, the exchange market gradually loosened, and half a yuan for June could be settled, leading to a downward trend. Later, banks tightened, retreating to within $29.80. Securities: Public Bonds Under the Shadow of Rumors

Silver Industry Sells Off, Downturn Intensifies

Yesterday, at the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange, the trend of public bonds suddenly became unstable. The Japanese invaded Tianjin, and rumors were rampant, but they had not been verified. The market air was suddenly tense. Most people still could not avoid being influenced by unfounded rumors, and sellers crowded the market. Among them, No. 46 sold off more actively. The rest were mostly retail investors. The Northern Group did not have large entries or exits. In the morning, the Disbandment bond still rose by 1 jiao. However, because the volume of sales increased more and more later, the market price fell more and more sharply. The Salt Tax fell by as much as 9 jiao. Because No. 46 was close to the financial circles, its long positions may have had considerable reason to exit. Therefore, in the next round, retail investors also followed suit in droves. The troop cut plummeted by 1 yuan 2 jiao and a half in an instant. The 19 Customs and the 19 Charity also fell by 1 yuan. After that, because the fall in the first round had been significant, the downward trend slowed slightly, with the more falling by half a yuan and the less only by 1 jiao. Although there were many rumors in the market, they still could not be verified. In the afternoon, most short sellers took advantage of the small rebounds to cover their positions. The initial photography was still flat. Starting with the far-term troop cut, it gradually trended upward and became more vigorous later. Buyers suddenly increased, and the market price rose by 3 to 5 jiao. Before the closing, the various types listed still had more entries than exits, rising another 3 to 4 jiao. Afterwards, there were temporary rumors, and sellers again occupied the majority. Starting from the 20 Customs, they returned to fatigue. Generally, they fell back by 2 to 3 jiao. As a result, they all fell sharply, from several jiao to 1 yuan 2 to 3 jiao. The trend seemed to be discouraging. If the Tianjin incident is not resolved, there will be many more storms ahead. This Month's Flour Resale Decline

Yesterday morning's opening of the flour market saw all months generally fluctuate in a flat and weak range. With quotes for foreign wheat, both US and Canadian wheat were down a dime or two, creating instability in the market. Many outside investors engaged in buying and selling across near and far terms, which resulted in brisk trading but a flat and stable market. Until the afternoon session, the long position holders of the Customer guild for this month gradually resold because the factories had abundant chips and found it difficult to support the price. The minimum opening was 1.276 yuan. The major factories were not active in the long-term months, but the smaller factories slightly sold out, causing the market to continue to be sluggish. The current stagnation of buying interest is due to the increasing national crisis and tight monetary policy. If supply continues to exceed demand, the market will likely remain weak and lifeless. As a result, this month was down 5 li compared to the previous day, April/May down 2.5 li, June down 5 li, and July/August down 2.5 li.

Jinshan branches have been scarce in recent arrivals, and existing stock is dwindling, with some merchants holding firmly. Market trends are becoming increasingly tight. According to information from the area, only 40% of this year's flowering is expected, further strengthening the market. Yesterday, merchants were quoting top-grade Yuan branches at 27.5 taels, medium grade at 25 to 22 taels, top-grade flat branches at 34.2 taels, and lower grades at 29 taels. Glutinous rice branches are the scarcest, with good quality broken rice sticks now quoted at 100 taels.

Metals: Extreme Shortage of 6-Fen Road Leather in Stock

Six-fen road leather (packaging iron sheets) have recently been extremely scarce in the market, leading to a bullish sentiment and rising prices. Overseas orders are unlikely to arrive soon, which is expected to further raise the price.

League of Nations and the Four-Power Pact

France Advocates Within the League of Nations

Loyal Cooperation Among the Four Major European Powers

MacDonald Expresses Willingness to Accommodate the French Government's Views

Mussolini's Plan Appears to Have Been Revised

Reuters, Paris, 21st – The British Embassy released a statement tonight regarding the discussions between the Prime Ministers and Foreign Ministers of Britain and France, stating that the French authorities wished to establish loyal cooperation among the four major European powers—the permanent members of the League of Nations—for the sake of peace, within the structure and spirit of the League of Nations. French Prime Minister Daladier and Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour thanked the British authorities for the information provided, which allowed for a closer study of the British-Italian proposals, and promised to exchange views with each other as soon as possible.

MacDonald's Declaration

Absolutely No Intention to Harm the League of Nations

The British-French discussions began at 11:30 this morning and ended at 6:00 PM. After the French Prime Minister and others left the British Embassy, the above statement was released. British Prime Minister MacDonald told reporters after the meeting that Britain was not bound by any pre-set disarmament plan, nor was it bound by any plan to revise the peace treaty as a result of the meeting with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. When asked whether any plans to maintain peace in Europe had been drafted in Rome, the British Prime Minister replied that many proposals had indeed been discussed, but the Rome plan reported in the newspapers was not accurately based on facts. There were many rumors, and he refused to deny them. There was absolutely no intention to replace the League of Nations with the cooperation of the four major powers—Britain, France, Germany, and Italy—mentioned in the Rome communiqué.

Britain and France Issue a Joint Communiqué

Havas, Paris, 21st – The French Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the British Embassy jointly issued a communiqué to the press, stating that British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Minister Simon had come to Paris from Rome to report to French Prime Minister Daladier and Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour on the nature of their meeting with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini in Rome. The British and French authorities reported in detail to the French government, allowing it to study the Italian proposal in the long term, which was deeply appreciated. In the near future, the authorities of the two countries will continue to exchange views. The French cabinet members hope to promote sincere cooperation among the four major powers—the permanent members of the League of Nations Administrative Council—within the spirit and scope of the League of Nations to seek peace in Europe.

British and French Consultations Are Extremely Cordial

Havas, Paris, 21st – British Prime Minister MacDonald, Foreign Minister Simon, French Prime Minister Daladier, Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour, and others met at the British Embassy from 11:30 AM to 1:10 PM and then paused briefly. The British cabinet members reported to the French authorities on the British-Italian talks in Rome. The discussions were extremely cordial. At 3:00 PM, key figures from Britain and France began to study the contents of the British-Italian plan again, concluding at 5:45 PM. Daladier and Paul-Boncour declined to make a statement on the British-French talks, only saying that a communiqué would be issued at 6:30 PM.

Disarmament Conference Will Be Temporarily Suspended

Havas, Geneva, 21st – After consulting with the Presidium, Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson decided to recommend to the General Committee at its meeting on Thursday that the Disarmament Conference be temporarily suspended until after Easter. As the Italian Prime Minister's proposal is still under negotiation between Britain and France, the Disarmament Conference must be temporarily suspended.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 22nd – Finance Minister Takahashi visited Prime Minister Saito at the Prime Minister's official residence in Nagatacho at 9:00 AM today for important talks. Japan Federation, Tokyo, 22nd – Recently, various parties have demanded the establishment of an agency like the Diplomatic General Staff Headquarters to decide on national policies regarding diplomacy and quickly resolve diplomatic issues. For this purpose, it is absolutely necessary to establish a large agency like the Diplomatic Investigation Committee and implement strong diplomacy. Opening of the New National Assembly Announces

Germany Establishes a New Military State

The End of the Weimar Constitution Era

Reuters, Berlin, 22nd – When the National Assembly reconvenes tomorrow, the National Socialist Party and its fellow parties will put forward an important motion to grant the government full executive powers for a period of four years, with President Hindenburg having the power to intervene in the government. The motion contains five articles: 1. The government has the power to enact laws, including budget bills and the approval of laws. 2. Such laws may deviate from the Constitution if they do not harm the National Assembly and Federal Council or harm the President's rights. 3. Such laws shall be drafted by the Prime Minister and shall take effect on the day of promulgation, provided that Articles 68 and 77 of the Constitution shall not hinder such laws. 4. Treaties concluded with foreign countries regarding German legal matters do not need to be approved by the National Assembly or the Federal Council. 5. The motion shall take effect on the day of promulgation and expire on April 1, 1937, or on the day of the replacement of the current National Assembly.

Reuters, Potsdam, 21st – The German National Assembly held a solemn opening ceremony in Potsdam Church today, declaring that Germany would be transformed into a new military state stirred by the old military spirit of Prussia. President Hindenburg, Prime Minister Hitler, and the deposed Crown Prince were all central figures in the meeting. Although the throne in the church was empty, the respect of the Allied Powers for the royal family could still be seen in the two salutes given by President Hindenburg to the deposed Crown Prince before and after the ceremony. President Hindenburg addressed the National Assembly, warning that the responsibility before you is great and complex, and I hope that all members of the new National Assembly will dedicate their loyalty to assist the government. The place where we stand today will make us never forget that Prussia's greatness was due to fearing God and fulfilling our duties, being courageous in our work, and being loyal and patriotic.

Havas, Berlin, 21st – The House of Representatives, elected on March 5th, held its second meeting this afternoon at the Kroll Opera House. The ambassadors of France and Poland and the deposed Crown Prince, dressed in brilliant uniforms, also attended the ceremony. Prime Minister Hitler took his seat at 5:12 PM, and the audience applauded in welcome. At 5:15 PM, former Speaker Goering announced the opening of the meeting and immediately elected the Speaker and Deputy Speakers. Goering was re-elected as Speaker, Esser of the Centre Party was elected as First Deputy Speaker, Graf of the National Right Party was elected as Second Deputy Speaker, and Sörensen of the National Socialist Party was elected as Third Deputy Speaker. Speaker Goering delivered an opening speech, stating that Germany had recovered the spirit of Frederick the Great and that the era of the Weimar Constitution had ended. He also said that today was the anniversary of the opening of the first German Diet in 1871, and that the opening of this session of the House of Representatives on this day was very gratifying. Goering also paid tribute to President Hindenburg in the name of the House of Representatives and then swore allegiance to Prime Minister Hitler. The National Socialist Party and the National Right Party all cheered enthusiastically, but the Centre Party and the Social Democratic Party showed no reaction. The House of Representatives then adjourned until Thursday.

Reuters, Berlin, 21st – The new National Assembly began its work in the grand theater here tonight, lasting only 40 minutes. Goering was re-elected as Speaker and then, after transferring the resolution proposed by the Social Democratic Party requesting the release of the arrested members of the party to the committee for review, the National Assembly announced an adjournment until March 23rd.

Reuters, Berlin, 22nd – An emergency decree will be submitted to President Hindenburg for signature today, which stipulates the following: 1. A general amnesty for political prisoners whose crimes were committed out of loyalty to the country. 2. Anyone who maliciously attacks the government, participates in national revolutions, non-party members who possess party uniforms, spreads inaccurate or far-fetched news that seems to harm the happiness of the country or the honor of the central and federal governments shall be sentenced to imprisonment or hard labor. These crimes will be tried at any time by special courts. The decree also stipulates that anyone who wears party uniforms without qualification and commits a crime with the purpose of terrorizing the people or causing disputes with foreign governments may be sentenced to death at the most severe.

Page 18

Convene a Pacific Conference

To Resolve the Sino-Japanese Issue

Advocated by Seiyukai Member Ashida

(Havas, Tokyo Correspondence, March): Dr. Ashida, the chairman of the Japan Times, is an old diplomat and an influential figure in the Seiyukai. During the recent session of the Imperial Diet, Ashida raised questions, accusing Japanese diplomacy of being dictated by the military. When this case was raised, people in Geneva discussed it, and then so did people in Japan.

Ashida recently published an article in the Japan Times, outlining the basis for Japan's new policy based on his own views.

Dr. Ashida said that Japan, due to its discord with Geneva, has decided to disregard the countries of the world and adopt a completely independent policy. However, it does not know that various things in the international economy, culture, and geography are interconnected. If this relationship is not changed one day, no country can isolate itself from the world. If it must be done, it is to return to the Tokugawa era and completely lose the status of a great power that has been painstakingly acquired.

In addition, Japan cannot give up much of its established policy toward Manchuria. The recognition of Japan's special rights in Manchuria is not a problem at present. This is because such rights were recognized by the powers before the European War. Former British Foreign Secretary Lord Curzon informed the Japanese government that Britain recognized Japan's superior position in the Far East. In 1917, U.S. Secretary of State Lansing also declared to Japanese Ambassador Ishii Viscount that the United States recognized that Japan had special interests in Manchuria. (Editor's note: The Lansing-Ishii Agreement has been cancelled successively with the Anglo-Japanese Alliance, and the above statements are no longer valid.) Therefore, the current problem is not here.

In short, the goal of Japan and the League of Nations is the same: (to maintain peace in the Far East). The only difference is the method of achieving this goal. Japan believes that Manchuria's separation from China and its establishment as an independent country is an indispensable condition for maintaining peace in the Far East, while the League of Nations holds the opposite view. What the League of Nations is arguing for is form, while Japan emphasizes reality.

However, the reason for the conflict between Japan and the League of Nations is not entirely the Manchurian problem. Japan's clumsy diplomacy and failure to adapt to changing circumstances are the biggest reasons.

The current situation cannot be allowed to continue like this for a long time. This situation must be broken. To achieve this goal, Japan's policy must be reformed based on the following points:

1. Japan should strive to delay other countries' decisions for three or four years. After this period, Manchuria can be developed and (Manchukuo) can be stabilized.

2. After three or four years, the relationship between China and (Manchukuo) should improve, and the current difficulties will naturally disappear.

3. Although Japan is determined to defend (Manchukuo), it has no ambition to invade Chinese territory or Siberia. Japan should compromise with China and the Soviet Union to guarantee the borders of (Manchukuo) on this level.

4. The chaotic situation in China poses a long-term danger to Sino-Japanese relations and peace in the Far East. This point has been recognized in the Lytton Report. Japan should cooperate sincerely to consolidate the central government of China and assist it in its struggle against the Communist Party and bandits with the same mentality.

5. Every effort should be made to completely eliminate the misunderstanding between Japan and the United States. The origin of this misunderstanding is mostly due to American public opinion, which mistakenly believes that Japan has the ambition to invade territory in China, or even Siberia. Attempts should be made to dispel it.

Ashida advocated convening a conference in Tokyo of countries related to the Pacific in order to determine Japan's new policy based on the above principles.

The agenda for this conference is roughly as follows:

1. To consolidate the central government of China through international cooperation.

2. To sign arbitration and friendship treaties by countries along the Pacific coast, including Soviet Russia, China, (Manchukuo), Japan, and the United States.

3. To discuss Japan's proposed naval disarmament plan. Ashida believes that the greatest difficulty is to get China to participate in this conference, and the Japanese diplomatic authorities should work hard to achieve this.

The Soviet Union's National Defense in the Five-Year Plan (Continued)

The Red Army did not have tanks before either. During the civil war, the dozens of tanks captured from the White Army and interventionists could not actually be counted as tank weapons. But before 1929, these dozens of tanks were the only samples used to train the Red Army. When reviewing the Red Army, we would often display these dozens of tanks, and foreigners would often laugh to themselves when they saw them. However, the significance of tanks in modern warfare is extremely important. Machine guns are deployed across the entire line, and they cannot be broken through without the use of tanks. This is why the armies of various countries are paying close attention to tanks. At the same time, the armies of various countries are making efforts to study the various functions of tank technology and strategy, and this is also the reason.

What was even more difficult was that before 1928, the Soviet Union had absolutely no technical personnel who could manufacture tanks themselves, whether in the automobile industry or the tractor manufacturing industry, let alone anything else. Therefore, we first had to imitate foreign tank styles. As a result of our efforts, we can now manufacture new-style tanks. Not only can we manufacture them ourselves, but we have also established a foundation for manufacturing tanks and trained skilled craftsmen. Now, we can also say without exaggeration that during the four years of the first five-year plan, we have completely learned new-style tank weapons in manufacturing and military applications.

Regarding the air force, let me say a few words. The Soviet Union's air force was not weak before 1928. Great progress has been made both before and at the beginning of the first five-year plan. However, in terms of the quality of aircraft, such as flight altitude and payload, it could not keep up with the world's aviation technology. During the four years of the first five-year plan, the Soviet Union's aircraft manufacturing industry did make great progress. The Soviet Union invented several new types of aviation engines, which are now being manufactured in large quantities. A lot of aviation talent has also been trained. We believe that during the second five-year plan, the Soviet Union will definitely catch up with the world's aviation technology level, and even surpass it.

As for the navy, the five-year plan naturally did not take it lightly. During the four years, all fleets were repaired, and some were thoroughly renovated. The submarine fleet was also strengthened, and coastal defense was greatly consolidated. The number of naval personnel has increased greatly, and their knowledge and naval skills have improved compared to before. Needless to say, the shipbuilding industry has also developed.

All of this technological transformation of the Red Army's armaments was not only not an easy task for us military personnel, but also cost the country a lot. What we are talking about here is still the expenditure used for the Red Army's armaments technology. The expenditure used to create the foundation for the military industry is not included. In 1927-28, the amount of money used for technology was already considerable, and during the five-year plan, the cost of implementing the transformation of armaments was naturally even greater. However, it was precisely because of this that the Red Army was able to be thoroughly transformed technologically, so that the Red Army was not only greatly consolidated in terms of revolutionary spirit, organization, and military discipline, but also incomparably consolidated in terms of Soviet military technology (including complex military technologies such as the air force and tanks).

Finally, let me briefly talk about the Red Army's cadres. The modernization of military technology naturally requires a large number of technical personnel, engineers, and officers with commercial and military knowledge. The training institution for officers is the Army University. In 1928, there were a total of 3,198 students in all Army Universities. In 1932, the various Army Universities were specialized, and the number of students increased even more, and various methods were adopted to strengthen the training of military instructors. In recent years, the results in this area will be fully demonstrated.

However, the reform of military technology not only requires senior officers, but also requires middle and lower-ranking officers. During the five-year plan, all military schools in the Soviet Union were greatly reformed, and many new military specialized schools were established, such as aviation, tanks, and logistics.

During the first five-year plan, what changed in the army itself was the re-deployment of company and platoon leaders. This was to adapt to the technological transformation of the Red Army. For example, the number of infantry officers was slightly reduced, as was the cavalry. On the contrary, the number of artillery teams, tank teams, and other engineers and officers has increased greatly.

The social composition of officers has also been greatly improved. In 1928, workers accounted for 28%, and in 1932, this had increased to 40%. The number of party members among officers has also increased greatly. In 1928, it was 55%, and in 1932, it had increased to 61%. In particular, the number of party members among senior and important military personnel has increased even more. For example, among artillery officers, the percentage increased from 15% to 81% during the same period, and among infantry officers, it increased from 54% to 88%. The entire armored car force was composed of party members.

The number of Communist Youth League members (the party's reserve army) in the Red Army has increased even faster. In 1928, party members and youth league members accounted for 31.6% of all Red Army soldiers and officers. Now, this has increased to 59.4%. The general cultural level of Red Army soldiers, officers, and political workers has also greatly improved. The army has also established combat training classes and various lecture groups to cultivate the military and political lives of officers and soldiers. (Translated from Izvestia, January 24, 1933)

Tian Jun Recovers Bazhong

Bandits Fleeing Towards Qingjiangdu

Only Bloodstains and Abandoned Corpses Seen in the City

Sichuan Correspondence: The red bandits in Bazhong have been repeatedly attacked fiercely by the National Army under Tian Songyao's command. Despite repeated setbacks, they have stubbornly defended themselves. On March 9, a battalion of bandits came to Xishan to surrender, strongly stating that the red bandits were internally shaken and lacked bullets. According to reconnaissance reports, it was also said that the bandit army was surrounded on three sides by the National Army, making it difficult to advance or retreat. They were at their wit's end, and in addition, their food was running out. They intended to make a final desperate struggle, but if they failed, they would immediately flee elsewhere. After receiving the news, Zeng and Luo divisions of Tian's command dispatched elite troops from the Maobitan Fort and the Ya Pass at dawn on the 10th to attack in separate directions. They also first ordered Xue's regiment to cross the river from Lianghekou to threaten Wangwang Mountain. Song Peigen's regiment guarded the original line with a part of its troops, and personally led a part of its troops to fiercely attack the bandits in Bazhong City. The officers and soldiers, because they had been in a stalemate for a long time, were unusually angry, so they were all fearless and invincible. The bandits were also extremely stubborn and fought desperately. Short-range melee combat was very fierce. Finally, at 9 a.m., the bandits were repelled and Bazhong City was completely occupied. The red bandits fled in droves towards Jianshanping, Qingjiangdu, and Silin Bridge. The National Army also followed closely, capturing and killing many. Song's regiment then occupied Wangwang Mountain, and Zhu's regiment occupied Chaqi Mountain and Tazi Mountain, clearing out the bandits in the area near Bazhong City. Zeng's division sent Li Weiruo to command the troops and Liao's brigade to cross the river from Sanhekou and Shi Temple to advance and occupy Zhenzi Ya. Zeng's regiment occupied Daliang Mountain and Leigu Village, cooperating to encircle and suppress the remnant bandits. After the National Army entered Bazhong City, the remaining civilians were all delighted and encouraged, and stood on the roadside to welcome them. When asked about the red bandits' devastation, they all said that the food had been completely searched by the bandits. The people who remained in the county were either killed by the red bandit authorities or abused by the red bandits. The various sufferings were unbearable to hear. As for the houses, half of them were destroyed, and the market was also extremely desolate. What was reflected in the eyes were only the red bandit slogans between the walls, the mottled bloodstains in the streets and alleys, and the piles of abandoned corpses under the city and in the fields. (March 12)

Aviation Association Establishes Aviation School

School Site Has Been Negotiated

Borrowing Hongqiao Airport

The Chinese Aviation Association will establish an aviation school to develop China's aviation industry and train civil aviation personnel. This proposal has been planned for a long time. Regarding the issue of the school site, the directors of the association all believe that Shanghai is a suitable place. Because Shanghai is the most developed commercial port in China, it is convenient to hire professors and purchase equipment. The headquarters of the Aviation Association is also in Shanghai, so managing the school will not be isolated. However, Shanghai lacks a large site for practice. After discussion by the Standing Committee, it was decided to borrow the Hongqiao Airport of the Aviation Administration and to temporarily borrow the Administration's training aircraft for teaching. Therefore, the association specially sent its Secretary-General, Lin Wojiang, to Hangzhou to negotiate with Ge Jingen, the Director of the Aviation Administration. Lin returned to Shanghai last night. The reporter made a special visit to inquire about the progress of the negotiation. According to him, Director Ge has already agreed to borrow the site, but the matter of borrowing training aircraft is still under negotiation. Therefore, a meeting of the Standing Committee will be convened within days to report on the progress of the negotiation, and then a plan of action will be discussed. Director Ge is very concerned about the association, so he also offered suggestions to establish a machine factory, starting with a small scale, regardless of whether it is self-made or repaired, and striving to achieve the goal of self-manufacturing and self-repair. This idea is very good, so it will be reported to the Standing Committee for discussion.

Northeast Opens for Thawing and Navigation Today

Huge Amount of Grain Transported

Two Million Bags of Wheat Flour

Forty to Fifty Thousand Bags of White Rice

Yingkou and Andong in the Northeast have been closed to navigation for more than three months since the winter freeze. Today, thawing will begin, and Shanghai merchant ships will resume navigation to Yingkou starting today. However, at the beginning of this thawing and opening of navigation, a large amount of rice and flour suddenly went to the puppet state from Shanghai. This matter is not only related to people's livelihood, but also violates the ban. This newspaper reporter went to various places to investigate the details as follows:

Ordering Large Quantities of Flour and Rice

At this time of Japanese mobilization to attack Rehe, the front line needs a huge amount of food. It is said that the Japanese army eats white rice, while the puppet Manchurian army eats wheat flour. Therefore, recently, the Northeast has come to Shanghai to purchase a large amount of wheat flour, up to more than two million bags, mostly Green Soldier Brand. They also secretly purchased 40,000 to 50,000 bags of white rice. The destination of the transportation is divided into two places. Before Yingkou thawed, it was loaded to Dalian. Now that Yingkou has thawed, it is directly transported from Shanghai to that port for unloading. Various Shanghai Chinese and British merchant ships are competing to load them, including Haichang, Yu Da, Taifeng, Datong, Zhaoxing, Zhengji, and Taikoo.

Navigation Starts Today

A telegram from Yingkou said that the port there has thawed and is scheduled for the 25th of this month. Shanghai ships will start loading cargo to Yingkou today. Datong Company's Tongshun ship will transport 2,400 bags of white rice and 104,000 bags of wheat flour today. Taikoo's Zhejiang ship will also carry more than 100,000 bags of wheat flour. Taifeng's Fengxiang will also start operating today. According to the Jianghai Customs, it has long prohibited the transportation of food to the Northeast, and the Ministry of Communications has also instructed the various shipping bureaus not to load food to the Anyinglian ports of the puppet state. However, the general ships and vehicles are all turning a deaf ear to the order and competing to carry it. It is not known how the customs will handle it.

Forcing Crew Members to Register

When Yingkou and Andong were closed to rivers in the winter, the puppet state issued a fake order stating that when Chinese merchant ships sailed to the puppet state's seaports, in addition to paying taxes and banknotes upon entry, it also added that Chinese ships sailing to Yingkou and Andong must have the puppet customs inspect the ships and issue an inspection certificate before they can sail. It also ordered all Chinese ships entering Yingkou to register their crew members with the puppet state, paying a registration fee of two yuan or five yuan per person, which is the same as our country's regulations. This time, it will be forced to implement it.

Strict Inspection Situation

Dalian has prohibited the import of Shanghai Chinese newspapers. If anyone carries them, they will be heavily fined once they are found. Chinese people going to Dalian or Yingkou Andong from Shanghai must undergo a special search. In addition to unloading and inspecting luggage and items one by one, even the edges and linings of clothes and the linings of hats on the head must be opened on the spot with a knife and inspected by Japanese agents, and viewed against the sunlight. If there is any discrepancy, they will be considered spies and arrested, and their lives will be difficult to protect.

Disarmament Conference

Actually Restricts Our Development of the Air Force

China's Number of Aircraft is Only One-Fifth of Japan's

Makes Us Incapable of Self-Defense and Should Resolutely Oppose

The World Disarmament Conference has fallen into a stalemate due to the issue of restricting air forces. Recently, British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon proposed standards for restricting air forces, the content of which is that the five major powers, Britain, the United States, France, Italy, and Japan, shall not exceed 500 aircraft, and the rest shall be reduced in turn. China is actually restricted to no more than 100 aircraft. The Disarmament Conference will be held tomorrow (23rd). It is not known whether the proposal can be passed or whether it can be implemented after it is passed. However, it is deeply noteworthy for the Chinese people amidst the aviation salvation movement. Lin Wojiang, Secretary-General of the Aviation Association, told the Xin Sheng News Agency reporter this morning that China has an extremely long coastline and vast borders, and the equipment of the army and navy cannot be compared with that of the powers. If the air force is further restricted, it will be no different from placing our country in a position where it cannot defend itself, which the Chinese people should resolutely oppose. China's air force today is still less than a hundred aircraft. Whether it can build an air force sufficient for self-defense depends on the efforts of the Chinese people and the government, but there is a huge difference between this and being restricted internationally and thus unable to establish it.

Ministry of Industry and Fisheries Association

Levy Fisheries Construction Fee

Collection Rules Have Been Approved and Promulgated by the Ministry

The Provisional Rules for Levying Fisheries Construction Fees by the Fisheries Improvement Committee of the Ministry of Industry for the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Region: 1. These rules are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 3, Paragraph 2 of the organizational regulations of this committee. 2. The levy rate for fisheries construction fees is 2% of the market value of the catch, limited to one-time collection. 3. All catches, whether fresh, salted, dried, or shellfish, shall pay fisheries construction fees in accordance with these regulations. 4. The collection of fisheries construction fees for catches shall begin at 100 catties. Amounts less than this, or small-scale hawkers, shall be exempt. 5. The collection of fisheries construction fees shall be carried out by fish merchants on behalf of the government. When necessary, the Fisheries Improvement Committee of the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Region may establish offices for collection. Expenditures shall not exceed 5% of the fees collected. The collected fees shall be submitted to the Fisheries Improvement Committee of the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Region for safekeeping before the fifth day of the following month. 6. A four-part form shall be filled out for the collection of fisheries construction fees. One part shall be given to the fish merchant, one part shall be kept at the collection location, and two parts shall be submitted to the Ministry of Industry and the Fisheries Improvement Committee of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, respectively. The forms shall be pre-printed by the Ministry of Industry and stamped with the official seal of the Fisheries Improvement Committee of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. 7. Those who fail to report or report inaccurately shall be subject to penalties assessed by the collecting agency or inspectors, depending on the circumstances (the penalty rules will be formulated separately). 8. The detailed rules for the implementation of these rules shall be drafted by the committee and submitted to the Ministry of Industry for approval. 9. These rules shall take effect on the date of approval by the Ministry of Industry.

Cargo Transfer Business Shipping Slips

Ministry of Finance Approves Exemption from Stamp Duty

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce, according to the letter from the Cargo Transfer Business Association, requested that the Ministry of Finance approve the exemption of shipping slips from stamp duty. The chamber immediately forwarded the request for exemption. It is now learned that the Ministry of Finance has approved the request, stating: "We have received the submission. The shipping slips issued by the cargo transfer business are temporary slips given by the carrier company to the cart drivers to be presented to the store shipping the goods. They are not substitutes for bills of lading or official receipts. Since the bills of lading, etc., already comply with the regulations for stamp duty, these shipping slips should be exempt from stamp duty. In addition to instructing the Jiangsu Stamp and Alcohol Tax Bureau to comply, you are to notify them accordingly."

Abolition of the Confucius Temple Sweeping Bureau

The Confucius Temple on Confucius Temple Road, Xiaoximen, in this city, has traditionally had a Sweeping Bureau. The Municipal Bureau of Education, intending to use the Confucius Temple to establish a public education center, submitted a request to the Municipal Government for instructions on whether the Confucius Temple Sweeping Bureau should be abolished and how the bureau's assets should be handled. The Municipal Government then forwarded the request to the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Education for instructions. The Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Education have replied, stating: "Regarding the property of the Confucius Temple, the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Education, together with the Ministry of Finance, have formulated the Regulations for the Custody of Confucius Temple Property, which have been promulgated and implemented. The Confucius Temple Sweeping Bureau is no longer necessary and should be abolished within a time limit. The Confucius Temple property under its management should be received and managed by the local educational administrative authorities in accordance with the provisions of Article 3 of the Custody Regulations."

Newspaper Vendor Murdered

Zhou Yiting Dies Under a Sharp Axe

Zhou Yiting, a native of Nanjing, was fifty years old. He lived at No. 190, Shanqing Lane, Avenue Edward VII. He was a newspaper vendor. Because he had been in the business for many years, he had accumulated some savings. At the same time, he was quite respected among the newspaper vendors. However, Zhou did not rest on his laurels because of his age, and still went out every morning to manage everything. Unexpectedly, at about 6:00 AM this morning, just as Zhou was walking out of his house, several thugs suddenly jumped out from the side of Shanqing Lane, wielding sharp axes. Without asking any questions, they slashed Zhou five times in a row. After being attacked, Zhou cried out for help. When the nearby police arrived, the suspects had already fled. The Chinese police officer No. 1782 reported the incident to the police station, which dispatched a vehicle to rush Zhou to Tongren Hospital for treatment. However, due to the severity of his injuries, he died in the hospital at 9:00 AM. The hospital reported the death to the police station, which sent the body to the morgue for examination. At the same time, the police station dispatched detectives to search for the suspects. It was learned that Zhou suffered five axe wounds, three to the head and two to the shoulder. The three wounds to the head were the most fatal.

Acquittal in the Bizarre Case of Encouraging Shaved Heads

Failure to Find Evidence of a Crime

Lu Wenbin, a native of Pudong, has recently been enticing unemployed vagrants on various roads, claiming to recommend certain occupations, requiring them to shave their heads. Those who were deceived obeyed. Therefore, the number of beggars with shaved heads seen on the road recently has suddenly increased. Wu Ren'en, Tang Rongzhang, and others were all deceived and became suspicious of Lu. They successively reported to the police station, which detained Lu and sent him to the First Special District Local Court for a hearing. The court ordered him to be detained pending further investigation. It was reported in the previous newspaper. It is now learned that after the police station detained Lu, they immediately began an investigation. Although his actions were suspicious and his behavior bizarre, no evidence sufficient to constitute a crime was found. He only induced people to shave their heads and a strange copper coin suspected of being a symbol of a traitor was found on him. This could not be considered evidence. Therefore, when the police lawyer Ru Bao Yi continued the hearing of the case this morning, he appeared in court to explain the investigation, saying that the police station did not advocate prosecution. Judge Feng then ordered Lu Wenbin to be released.

Continuing to Capture the Culprits of the Nanyang Labor Unrest

Inside the factory of Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company at No. 269 Broadway Road, a foreman in the tobacco leaf department named Zhang Desheng suddenly incited a riot on Monday morning of this week, gathering fifty to sixty workers who were incited to join him. They swarmed into the tin-packaging department on the third floor and rioted, wielding weapons and violently assaulting the factory staff members Li Zhitang, Li Yongyao, and the carpenter Chen Ronggui, who was trying to mediate, causing injuries. The Huishan Police Station, upon hearing the alarm, immediately dispatched Chinese and foreign detectives to the scene to stop the disturbance and arrested Zhang Desheng, the ringleader. The three injured, Li Zhitang, etc., were sent to the hospital for treatment. The situation was finally calmed down. The next morning, the police station sent Zhang to the First Special District Local Court for a hearing on the 28th of this month. Yesterday morning, when Zhang was being interrogated in court, representatives from both labor and management were present in court to listen. Wu Shiyuan, a worker who had supported Zhang Desheng, was also in the audience. Hong Haiquan, the director of the tin-packaging department, who had been summoned to testify, caught sight of him. Hong reported to the Chinese and foreign detectives in charge of the case that Wu was actually a perpetrator at the scene. Therefore, as the crowd was leaving the courtroom after Zhang's case was heard, Wu Shiyuan was detained by the police station. Under questioning, Wu confessed that Li A Jin, a native of Tongzhou, was also one of the culprits. Thus, Li was also arrested. This morning, Wu and Li were sent to the First Special Court, where Judge Wu Zehan interrogated them. Nanyang Company's representative lawyer Wu Linkun appeared in court to explain everything, while the police lawyer Zhang Tianyin requested that the case be postponed to the 28th, so that it could be merged with Zhang Desheng's case. Judge Wu immediately approved the request. After briefly questioning the two defendants, Wu and Li, he ordered them to be detained and postponed the hearing.

Talk

Credit

— Ji

Yesterday, this newspaper reported that several Swedish children pooled their money to remit funds to a factory in Italy to purchase hand-cranked organs. When there was no news, they jointly wrote to Prime Minister Mussolini. Mussolini not only sent the goods as requested, but also attached a personal letter explaining that the factory had gone bankrupt and apologizing to the children. We live in this world (denying responsibility like someone pointing at a cow's head after stealing it), (saying white lies without blushing). To actually hear such an unprecedented, world-shattering, miraculous event is truly surprising and admirable. We are speechless and cannot retract our astonishment!

The practice of remitting money to buy goods and then receiving (no news) is not considered a particularly (remarkable rare event) in our esteemed country, which is known as the (land of etiquette and righteousness, where credit is fundamental). It is not worth being surprised by. However, for a monster whose power is enough to shake the world, the authoritarian Mussolini of the Fascists, to know that the bankruptcy of a factory in his own country affects the nation's own position, dignity, and credit, and to be willing to personally apologize to a few mischievous foreign children is truly shocking. Some people may not believe it is true. Look at our socialites replying to marriage proposals, they still need to hire a secretary to write the letter. How much more so a national leader managing countless affairs every day? Where would they have the free time and inclination to care about transactions (that have anything to do with dignity or credit)? Fundamentally, our children would never dare to boldly try to test the limits of a powerful figure. Perhaps it is possible, but only if they first prepare a sum of (bribes) and then write to purchase (children's airplanes). Only in this way would they have the hope of receiving a reply that would be (published in its entirety) in the newspaper!

However, to return to the subject, the sage has already said, "If a person is without trustworthiness, I do not know what he can do. A large cart without a yoke and a small cart without a crossbar will not work." Shang Yang, with great fanfare, ordered the people to move the wood from the south gate to the north gate and rewarded them with a large sum of money, only to establish the credit of (the law being followed when it is announced). This proves that (establishing oneself and the nation, credit is fundamental) is indeed a golden rule. Unfortunately, our Young Marshal Zhang's (giving foreigners whatever they want) creed cannot be denied. He did indeed establish credit with foreigners, but the subsequent two telegrams of (defending the border with blood and life) and (resolutely resisting to the death even with one gun and one bullet remaining) when Jehol was invaded seem to show that he was not afraid to casually lie to his own people. To the point that the sage scolded him as (I do not know what he can do). The most annoying thing is that, with an imperial decree, he once telegraphed his resignation, and after arriving in Shanghai, his confidants made a statement saying that Zhang had decided to leave Shanghai with his family for Europe and America in the short term. This was evidenced by the various shipping companies competing to attract his business. However, there were also rumors that he was still reluctant to leave (according to the confidant's statement on the 18th). This is truly embarrassing. However, it is not good to blame him. The ignorant people can only blame the fact that the checks issued by the great men have also been affected by the gloomy world situation, and even if they are discounted, they cannot be circulated.

Shop Clerk Communications

Preventing Stock Shortages in Stores

To the Esteemed Editor:

I am a salesperson (commonly known as a clerk), and my monthly salary is eighteen dollars. Others, besides their regular salary, perhaps have commissions, raises, bonuses, and other extra income. But what about us? Don't even mention extra income; it's already difficult to get the full regular salary! Why is that? Taking leave (whether for weddings, funerals, or illness) results in salary deductions; making mistakes on invoices means paying compensation. I wouldn't even bother about these, because taking leave means you weren't doing any work, and invoice errors are due to your own negligence. The most unjust thing is having to pay compensation for missing stock!

Sir, do you know? All our colleagues, as long as they are salespeople, are responsible for managing the stock. In departments with many items, each person has to manage over a hundred kinds. As long as there is a shortage, you must compensate for the full amount. The reason given is to prevent us from cheating or stealing. But how can we cheat? The goods sold are taken by trainees to wrapping staff, who verify them before wrapping. The invoices are also checked by auditors. Stock is counted and recorded every night, and accountants come to verify it the next day. At the end of each month, auditors conduct a major stocktake. So there is fundamentally no way to cheat. How can we steal? Upon entering the store, no personal belongings can be brought in. If you have any, you must deposit them at the staff storage area. When taking them out, they are inspected by the administrative staff. So, even with extraordinary abilities, there is no way to steal, right?

The reasons for stock shortages are nothing more than two types. One is the visits of thief "uncles," who take advantage of our busy and inattentive moments to display their "three-hand" skills, taking without asking. The other is errors in deliveries from the factory or shortages within the packages. However, the manager says, "Salespeople should have eyes everywhere and ears in all directions. If thief uncles steal, it means one of the directions wasn't watched. Not watching means weak ability. Those with weak abilities should not only pay compensation but should also not be given food." Factory delivery errors and shortages are due to errors in one's own procedures. Why not unpack and count each item? So this kind of error is a manifestation of laziness. People with laziness should not be kept on." Sir, when one person is serving seven or eight customers, on the one hand, they have to serve them attentively, and on the other hand, they have to watch in all directions to prevent thief uncles from using their skills. In reality, it is impossible to do. Counting each item in the package is also practically impossible. Imagine, for any type of goods, the factory sends at least three to five hundred dozens (because wholesale goods are also shipped from the retail department, so they must come in large quantities). If each dozen has to be unpacked and counted, unless one does nothing else all day, how can it be done? Alas! Colleagues sometimes have to pay twenty or thirty dollars in compensation for missing stock, working a whole month and still having to pay some extra. However, under the pressure of losing our jobs, no one dares to say no to the manager's official rhetoric. If there is anything, it is only to complain to you, sir. I wonder if you would be willing to shout out for us, the "bitter clerks"? I respectfully request your

Peace,

Clerk Qiu Chunzhong

Editor's Note: The above is Mr. Qiu's original letter. We have not modified a single word. Judging from the writing style of this letter, he is at least a high school graduate. And a top-notch graduate at that! He is now a clerk, busy all day long, and the price is only eighteen good silver dollars per month. This is somewhat meager. As for the management methods of this store, some are certainly good, but some places are too harsh. Deducting salary for leave is correct in principle, but it is truly unreasonable to deduct salary for leave due to weddings, funerals, or illness. Paying compensation for incorrect invoices is even more unquestionable. However, since the store employs auditors, it seems that the auditors should bear at least half of the responsibility. As for the errors that the auditors find, they can be passed on to the customers without having to pay compensation. Even if some warning is necessary, it may as well be recorded daily and used as a basis for evaluation. As for the shortage of goods in the store, it is indeed a serious issue. No one can say the manager is wrong in handling it seriously. However, holding the clerks fully responsible is certainly possible in stores with slow business and many employees. It is difficult for the store where Mr. Qiu works. We know that forcing people to do what is difficult is impossible. In such cases, it seems necessary to add some personnel to each department to specifically manage this matter.

("So, unless you treat Chao You to a meal today and he returns the favor tomorrow, you'll have nothing to talk about with him from the day after tomorrow!")
